aiśamādyantanirmuktamatiśobhanamādarāva ||
namāmi vigrahaṃ sāmvaṃ saṃsāraviṣabheṣajam || 1 ||
satrāvasāne saṃnadvāḥ sarvavedārthavedane ||
sarvalokahite yuktāḥ sārāsāravivekinaḥ || 2 ||
svādhyāyādhyayane yuktāḥ svasthacittāḥ suniścalāḥ ||
sarvopadravanirmuktāḥ sarvaśatruvivarjitāḥ || 3 ||
abhyāgatānāmārtānāmatithīnāṃ priyaṃvadāḥ ||
maitryā karuṇayā yuktāḥ kumatāvapyupekṣakāḥ || 4 ||
parapuṣṭau mahāprītāḥ prajñāmānavivarjitāḥ ||
gavāṃ śuśrūṣaṇe yuktā guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratāḥ || 5 ||
vṛddhasevābhisaṃpannā vedavitpūjane ratāḥ ||
ṛjavo mṛdavaḥ svasthāḥ sarvadvaṃdvavivarjitāḥ || 6 ||
rudrākṣamālābharaṇāḥ sitamasmāvaguṇṭhitāḥ ||
tripuṇḍāvalibhirdīptā jaṭāvalkalasaṃyutāḥ || 7 ||
liṅgārcanaparā nityaṃ śivasyāmitatejasaḥ ||
śivābhimānasaṃpannāḥ śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ || 8 ||
śivaśabdajapadhvastapāpapañjarasundarāḥ ||
saṃsāravipavṛkṣasya mūlacchedanatatparāḥ || 9 ||
śrautasmārta sadācārāḥ sarvagotrarpayo varāḥ ||
vyāsaprasādasaṃpannaṃ viśvajñānamahodadhim || 10 ||
viśvātmavedinaṃ sākṣādvidhvastabhavakānanam ||
smṛtvā bhaktyā mahātmānaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ sūtamuttamam ||11||
etasminnantare śrīmānmahākāruṇikottamaḥ ||
sarvajñaḥ sarvabhūtānāmabhīṣṭaphaladaḥ prabhuḥ || 12 ||
prādurāsīnmahātejā rātrau sūrya iva svayam ||
taṃ dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ sarve vismitā gadradasvarāḥ || 13 ||
praṇamya daḍavaḍūmau dattvā tasyā''sanaṃ varam ||
pādaprakṣālanaṃ kṛtvā śraddhayā parayā saha || 14 ||
gandhapuṣpādibhirdivyaiḥ pūṃjya puṇyavatāṃ varam ||
samāśvāsya ciraṃ kālaṃ prasannamukhapaṅkajam || 15 ||
papracchuḥ sarvavedārthaṃ prasannā bhāgyagauravāt ||
so'pi sūtaḥ svamācāryai smṛtvā śaṃbhuṃ jagadgurum || 16||
sarvavidyāmayīmīśāṃ sākṣādvighnavināyakam ||
ṣaṇmukhaṃ ca sadā śuddhaṃ praṇamya bhuvi daṇḍavat || 17 ||
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā munīnālokya suvratān ||
vaktumārabhate sūtaḥ sarvavedārthamuttamam || 18 ||
namāmi saṃsāramahāviṣauṣadham || 19 ||
namāmi nānāvidhalokavaibhavām || 20 ||
sarvavedārthapraśno nāma prathamo'dhyāyaḥ || 1 ||
sarvavedārthapraśno nāma prathamo'dhyāyaḥ || 1 ||
atha vakṣyāmi vedārthe śṛṇuta śraddhayā dvijāḥ ||
śraddhayā rahitaṃ sarve phalāya na kadācana || 1 ||
parāparavibhāgena vedārtho dvividhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||
vedārthaḥ paramaḥ sākṣātparātparataraṃ param || 2 ||
aparo dharmasaṃjñaḥ syāttatparamāptisādhanam ||
adharmaḥ parihārāya vedārthatvena bhaktitaḥ
gīyate muniśārdūlaiḥ kadācinna tu mukhyataḥ || 3 ||
adharmaparihāreṇa dharmastvavyākulo bhavet || 4 ||
avyākulena dharmeṇa śraddhayā'nuṣṭhitena tu ||
vedārthaḥ paramaḥ sākṣātsidhyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ || 5 ||
so'yaṃ svāparayā śaktyā baddhavatpratibhāsate ||
ekaiva paramā śaktirmāyā durghaṭakāriṇī || 6 ||
śivasyānantarūpā sā vidyayā tasya naśyati ||
yā vinaśyati sā māyā cinmātre parikalpitā ||7||
adhiṣṭhānāvaśeṣo hi nāśaḥ kalpitavastunaḥ ||
bhāvasyaiva hyabhāvatvaṃ nāśo'bhāvasya bhavataḥ ||
bhāvābhāvasvabhāvābhyāmanya eva hi kelpitaḥ || 8 ||
adhiṣṭhānasya nāśo na satyatvādeva sarvadā ||
sarvādhiṣṭhānamīśānaṃ paśyanneva vimucyate || 9 ||
īśānaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ vedāntaśravaṇādinā ||
jāyate parahaṃsasya yatermukhyādhikāriṇaḥ || 10 ||
nā''śramāntaraniṣṭhasya kramāttasyāpi jāyate || 11 ||
brahmalokamavāpnoti vanastho naiṣṭhiko'pi ca ||
gṛhasthaḥ pitṛlokaṃ ca śivajñānaṃ tu bhikṣukaḥ || 12 ||
tatrāpi prathamo bhikṣurjñānecchodayavādhakāva ||
mahāpāpādayatnena mucyate munipuṅgavāḥ || 13 ||
dvitīyaḥ śāntidāntyādijñānānecchāmavāpnuyāt ||
tṛtīyo'khilavedāntaśravaṇecchāmavāmuyāt || 14 ||
caturtho jñānamāproti vedāntaśravaṇena tu ||
sa eva karmasaṃnyāsī parahaṃsasamāśrayaḥ ||
anye kāmyaparityāgādvikṣukā iti kīrtitāḥ || 15 ||
parokṣaṃ brahmavijñānaṃ śābdaṃ deśikapūrvakam ||
buddhipūrvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dahati vahnivat || 16 ||
śābdaṃ brahmātmavijñānamaparokṣaṃ mahattaram ||
saṃsāranāśakaṃ proktaṃ tamasaścaṇḍabhānuvat || 17 ||
ato vijñānalābhāya parahaṃso bhaveddijaḥ || 18 ||
kuṭīcakāśca haṃsāśva tathā'nye ca bahūkāḥ ||
ye bhaviṣyanti te kuryuḥ prājāpatyeṣṭisaṃjñitām || 19 ||
āgneyeṣṭiṃ dvijāḥ kuryuḥ parahaṃsābhilāṣiṇaḥ ||
paścātraidhātavīṃ kuryuḥ sarve saṃyatamānasāḥ || 20 ||
ye'nāhitāgnayo viprāsteṣāṃ neṣṭirvidhīyate ||
svasvamagnau tu homaṃ te kuryuḥ śradvāpuraḥsaram ||
virajākhyairmahāmantrairājyena caruṇā'pi ca || 21 ||
hutaśeṣaṃ caruṃ sājyaṃ prāśyā''camyaiva sarpiṣā ||
pūrṇāhutiṃ punaḥ kuryuḥ praṇavenāgnijāyayā || 22 ||
sahāniṃ punarāmrāya ayaṃ te yonirṛtvijaḥ ||
iti mantreṇa kuryuste maipoccāraṇamādarāt || 23 ||
saṃnyāsādhvaryuṇā dattaṃ daṇḍaṃ kāpāyameva ca || 24 ||
parigṛhya guroḥ pādaṃ praṇamya śraddhayā saha ||
vedāntaśravaṇaṃ kuryurjñānārthaṃ bhikṣukottamāḥ || 25 ||
kāmyakarmaphale doṣaṃ viditvā pratiṣiddhavat ||
kāmyakarma rājaṃstulyo bhikṣuṇā phalato bhavet || 26 ||
na santi japyā mantrāśca parahaṃsasya sarvadā ||
trayīsāramimaṃ mantraṃ jaṃpennityaṃ samāhitaḥ ||
praṇavādaparaṃ jatthā kadā mukto bhaviṣyati || 27 ||
oṅkāraḥ sarvamantrāṇāmuttamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||
oṅkāreṇa lavenaiva saṃsārābdhi tariṣyati || 28 ||
umārdhavigraho devo rudraḥ satyādilakṣaṇaḥ ||
viṣṇvādayo'pi devāśca rudrasyāsyānvayena tu ||
kathaṃcitpraṇavasyārthā bhaviṣyanti na mukhyataḥ || 30 ||
yatibhirjñānasiddhyarthamavimuktaṃ mahattaram ||
sthānaṃ saṃsevanīyaṃ syāñcintanīyaṃ tathaiva ca || 31 ||
avimukte mahādevaḥ sākṣādiśveśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ||
upāsyamānaḥ suprīto jñānaṃ sākṣātprayacchati || 32 ||
avimukte mahādevamanupāsya vimuktaye ||
naraḥ kiṃcidipaṃ bhuktvā kṣunivṛttiṃ kariṣyati || 33||
tasmānmumukṣubhirbhaktyā jñānārthamavimuktakam ||
nadhibhūte tathā'dhyātme sevanīyaṃ tathaiva ca || 34 ||
śatarudriyasaṃjñastu mantro japyo mahattaraḥ ||
rudrajāpī vimucyeta mahāpātakapañjarāva || 36 ||
samyagjñānaṃ ca labhate tena mucyeta bandhanāt ||
anena sadṛśaṃ japyaṃ nāsti satyaṃ śrutau smṛtau || 37 ||
epā pañcākṣarī vidyā śatarudriyamadhyagā ||
pañcākṣare mahādevaḥ sarvadā supratiṣṭhitaḥ || 38 ||
mahādevasya sāṃnidhyādvyaṣṭibhūtāśva devatāḥ ||
tatra pratiṣṭhitā eva vṛkṣe śākhā yathā sthitāḥ || 39 ||
vṛkṣasya mūlasekena śākhāḥ puṣyanti vai yathā || 40 ||
śive rudrajapātprīte prītā evānyadevatāḥ ||
ato rudrajapādeva bhuktimuktī prasidhyataḥ || 41 ||
māyā māheśvarī śaktiḥ sattvādiguṇabhedataḥ ||
jīvamākramya saṃsāre bhrāmayatyaniśaṃ dvijāḥ || 42 ||
sattvātsukhaṃ ca jñānaṃ ca vairāgyaṃ śauklyameva ca || 43 ||
duḥkhapravṛttiḥ kāmaśca lauhityaṃ rajaso bhaveda ||
moho bhrāntistathā''lasyaṃ kāryaṃ ca tamaso bhavet ||44||
'evamuttamarūpāśca padārthāḥ sattvasaṃbhavāḥ ||
tathā madhyamarūpāśca padārthā rājasāḥ smṛtāḥ ||
vihīnāstāmasā eva padārthāḥ saṃgraheṇa tu || 45 ||
sattvādiguṇatrayaṃ kāryadvārā vyavacchinatti – sattvātsukhaṃ caiti || 43 ||
ato māyāmayaḥ sākṣātsaṃsāraḥ sarvadehinām ||
sa śivajñānamātreṇa sadya eva nivartate || 46 ||
jñānayajñena viprāṇāmāstikānāmamāninām ||
jāyate paramaṃ jñānaṃ nānyathā munipuṅgavāḥ || 47 ||
yajñaśca dvividhaḥ proktaḥ sthūlasūkṣmaṃvibhedataḥ ||
karmayajñaḥ samākhyātaḥ sthūlaḥ sarvārthavittamaiḥ ||
jñānayajño bhavetsūkṣmaḥ sākṣātsaṃsāravādhakaḥ || 48 ||
karmayajñābhidhaḥ sthūlastriprakāro vyavasthitaḥ ||
kāyiko vācikaścaiva mānasaśceti suvratāḥ || 49 ||
nityanaimittikādyastu kāyikaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||
mantrāṇāṃ japarūpastu vāciko vedavittamāḥ || 50 ||
devatādhyānarūpastu mānasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||
kāyikādādhikaḥ prokto vāciko matimattaḥ || 51 ||
mānaso vācikācchreṣṭha mānaso bahudhā smṛtaḥ ||
dhyeyabhedena so'pyevamuttamācamabhedataḥ || 52 ||
dvividhastatra devasya śivasya dhyānamuttamam ||
viṣṇvādīnāṃ tu devānāṃ dhyānaṃ cādhamamipyate || 53 ||
ato mokṣārthibhiḥ prājñaiḥ śiva aikaḥ śivaṃkaraḥ ||
dhyeyaḥ sarva parityajya śivādanyaṃ tu daivatam || 54 ||
. asminnarthe śrutiḥ sādhvī samāptā vedavittamāḥ || 55 ||
apakvacittairmokṣārthaṃ devā viṣṇvādayo'pi ca ||
dhyeyāḥ pakkaiḥ śivo dhyeyaḥ sākṣātsaṃsāramocakaḥ ||56||
rudraṃ viśvādhikaṃ viṣṇuṃ brahmāṇaṃ cānyameva vā ||
samaṃ saṃcintayansākṣātsaṃsāre parivartate || 57 ||
mahāpāpavatāṃ puṃsāṃ pūrvajanmasu suvratāḥ ||
viṣṇuḥ sarvādhiko bhāti na sākṣātparameśvaraḥ ||58||
viṣṇuḥ sarvādhiko bhāti nārakī sa na saṃśayaḥ ||
viṣṇuḥ sarvādhiko nāmya iti cintayatāṃ nṛṇām ||59||
nāsti saṃsāravicchittiḥ kalpakoṭiśatairapi ||
tepāṃ naiva ca mokṣāśā kalpakoṭiśatairapi || 60 ||
brahmādidevatānāṃ ca viśvādhikyaṃ vadanti ye ||
adhomukhordhvapādāste yāsyanti narakārṇavam || 61 ||
viṣṇorvā brahmaṇo vā'pi tathaivānyasya kasyacit ||
sāmyaṃ vadanti ye teṣāṃ na saṃsārādvimokṣaṇam || 62 ||
viṣṇuprajāpatīndrādidevatāsu munīśvarāḥ ||
vihīnāsu śivaṃ paśyanmucyate bhavabandhanāt || 63 ||
śivarudra mahādevabrahmeśānādināmataḥ ||
viṣṇvādidevatāḥ paśyankramānmucyeta bandhanāt || 64 ||
śivaṃ sarvottamaṃ viprā hariviṣṇvādināmataḥ ||
cintayanghorasaṃsāre patatyeva na saṃśayaḥ || 65 ||
yathā'mātyādibuddhistu rājñi bādhāya dehinām ||
tathā viṣṇvādibuddhistu śive vādhāya dehinām || 66 ||
ataḥ śivaḥ sadā dhyeyaḥ prādhānyena manīṣibhiḥ ||
jñānayajñātparo yajño nāsti nāsti śrutau smṛtau ||67||
jñānayajñaikaniṣṭhasya na kiṃcidapi durlabham ||
mahāpāpavatāṃ nṛṇāṃ jñānayajño na rocate || 68 ||
pratyuta jñānayajñastu pradeṣyo bhāsate svataḥ ||
viśuddhaṃ jñānamutpannaṃ yasya tasya mahātmanaḥ || 69 ||
śivarudramahādevabrahmeśānādināmasu ||
rudramūrtiṣu sarvāsu śāntidāntyādisādhane || 70 ||
tiryaktrapuṇḍre rudrākṣe tathā bhasmāvaguṇṭhane |
śivaliṅgasya prajāyāṃ śivasthāneṣu suvratāḥ || 71 ||
priyabuddhiḥ prajāyeta svabhāvādeva sarvadā ||
yasya vijñāninasteṣu prapo vā'pi jāyate ||
upekṣā vā na sa jñānī paśurvijñānavañcakaḥ || 72 ||
rutkarṣādityato viṣṇvādiṣu śivabuddhiryuktetyāha - viṣṇuprajāpatīti || 63 ||
sarvatra nāsti vidveṣaḥ sādhyasādhanapūrvake ||
sākṣāddijñānino viprā upekṣābuddhireva hi || 73 ||
tathā'pyukteṣu sarveṣu śaiveṣu dvijapuṅgavāḥ ||
priyabuddhiḥ svato bhāti vādhitākārarūpataḥ || 74 ||
bādhitākārato vā'pi yasya buddhiḥ svato na hi ||
epvasau naiva vijñānī bhrānta eva na saṃśayaḥ || 75 ||
karmāvalamvanenaiva kecijjīvanti mānavāḥ ||
jñānāvalambanenaiva jīvantyanye vimohitāḥ || 76 ||
anekakoṭibhiḥ kalperjñānayajñasya vaibhavam ||
mayā madguruṇā'nyairvā na śakyaṃ paribhāṣitum ||77||
tathā'pi munayaḥ śraddhāmātramāsādya kevalam ||
praśaṃsanti mahābhāgyājjñānayajñasya vaibhavam || 78 ||
aśaktā api vijñātuṃ jñānayajñasya vaibhavam ||
śraddhayā svādhikāreṇa vadanti jñānavaibhavam || 79 ||
punaḥ kaṇādakapilaprabhṛtīnāmapi svataḥ ||
doṣo na vidyate jñāne virodhe'pi parasparam || 80 ||
taistairnirūpitaṃ jñānaṃ vastuto naiva darśanam ||
upacāreṇa vijñānaṃ śraddhāpratatayā dvijāḥ || 81 ||
vyāsaḥ sākṣācchivajñānī śivasyaiva prasādataḥ || 82 ||
tatprasādādahaṃ sākṣācchivajñānī na saṃśayaḥ ||
mayā tatsaṃgraheṇaiva proktaṃ yuṣmākamādarāt || 83 ||
matprasādena vijñānayajñavaibhavamāstikāḥ ||
jñātavantaḥ kṛtārthāśca yūyaṃ satyamidaṃ vacaḥ || 84 ||
itaḥ pūrva mayā'nyeṣāṃ nāyamartho'bhibhāṣitaḥ ||
vyāso mama guruḥ pūrva rahasyaṃ me'bhyabhāṣata || 85 ||
sārātsārataraḥ sākṣādayamarthaḥ prabhāṣitaḥ ||
gopanīyastvayaṃ nityaṃ bhavadbhiḥ paramāstikaiḥ || 86 ||
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sutasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava-
dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ || 2 ||
nāma dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ || 2 ||
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi karmayajñasya vaibhavam ||
karmayajñavidhā prokto munibhiḥ sūkṣmadarśibhiḥ || 1 ||
ekaḥ kāmyo'paro nityastathā naimittiko'paraḥ ||
prādhānyena phalaṃ śuddhirārthikī kāmyakarmaṇaḥ || 2 ||
prādhānyena phalaṃ śuddhirnityasya phalamārthikam ||
kevalaṃ pratyavāyasya nivṛttiritarasya tu || 3 ||
kāmyarūpeṣu yajñeṣu yatante śraddhayā saha ||
mandabhāgyā narā viprā nityanaimittikātmaike ||
mahābhāgyāḥ pravartante teṣāṃ muktirayatnataḥ || 4 ||
vidhyuktamiti buddhayā ye vartante śraddhayā saha ||
aiṣu yajñeṣu sarveṣu teṣāṃ mandaphalaṃ bhavet || 5 ||
śivārādhanavṛddhayā ye yatante śraddhayā saha ||
eṣu yajñeṣu te śīghraṃ vimuktiphalamāpnuyuḥ || 6 ||
akartā'hamabhoktā'hamasaṅgo'hamahaṃ śivaḥ ||
iti vijñāya mānena svātmānaṃ tarkato'pi caṃ || 7 ||
karmayajñeṣu ye nityaṃ yatante śraddhayā'nvitāḥ ||
mahādevavijñānamaparokṣamavāpnuyuḥ || 8 ||
yajñarūpaṃ mahāviṣṇuṃ yajñe paśyanti ye dvijāḥ ||
te tu vijñānamāsādya kaivalyaṃ jñānamāpnuyuḥ || 9 ||
prādhānyena mahādevo yajñairijyo na cāparaḥ ||
iti jñātvā yajante ye te'pi vijñānamāpnuyuḥ ||10||
viṣṇuṃ brahmāṇamindraṃ vā devatāntarameva vā || 11 ||
pradhānabuddhayā ye yajñairyajante mohato'pi vā ||
te yānti narakaṃ ghoraṃ yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam || 12 ||
nāmataścārthato yastu mahādevo maheśvaraḥ ||
sa eva sāmbaḥ sarvajña ijyaḥ sarvamahāmakhaiḥ || 13 ||
yāni loke'niṣiddhāni karmāṇyavihitāni ca ||
tāni śaṃbho mahāpūjetye tajjñānaṃ mahāmakhaḥ || 14 ||
yāni karmāṇi sarvāṇi niṣiddhāni śrutau smṛtau ||
tāni cā''rādhanaṃ śaṃbhoriti jñānaṃ mahāmakhaḥ ||15||
īśvarārthadhiyā pāpānyapi karmāṇi suvratāḥ ||
bhavanti pūtānyatyantaṃ satyameva na saṃśayaḥ || 16 ||
ārdrakāṣṭhaṃ mahānagniḥ śuṣkaṃ kṛtvā dahedyathā ||
tatheśvaradhiyā pāpaṃ śuddhavijñānadaṃ bhavet || 17 ||
vidhyuktakarmaniṣṭhānāmiṣṭasya karaṇaṃ tu yat ||
so'pi sākṣānmahāyajñaḥ samyagjñānasya kāraṇam || 18 ||
vidhyuktakarmaniṣṭhānāmaniṣṭakaraṇaṃ tu yat ||
tanmahāpātakaṃ proktaṃ saṃsārasya pravartakam || 19 ||
durācāriṣu sarveṣu vinā doṣasya darśanam ||
upekṣāvṛddhirutpannoṃ so tasyāyaṃ mahāmakhaḥ || 20 ||
buddhārhatādimārgasthe devatāpratimāsu ca ||
devatābudvimātraṃ yatso'pi yajñaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || 21 ||
vaidikaṃ tāntrikaṃ hitvā mārga svaprajñayā dvijāḥ ||
yatra yo devatāvṛddhi karoti śradvayā saha || 22 ||
so'pi yajña iti prokto mayā vedārthavittamāḥ ||
śrayā sahitaṃ sarva śreyase bhūyase bhavet || 23 ||
svabuddhyā vedaśāstrokke tantrokte'pi dvijottamāḥ ||
āstikyaṃ devatābuddhirapi lābhāya dehinām ||24||
phaleṣu tāratamyaṃ tu vidyate sūkṣmadarśane || 25 ||
kāyikaḥ karmayajñastu kathitaḥ saṃgraheṇa tu ||
bhavanto'pi mahāyajñaṃ kāyikaṃ kuruta dvijāḥ || 26 ||
karmayajñavaibhavanirūpaṇaṃ nāma tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ || 3 ||
karmayajñavaibhavanirūpaṇaṃ nāma tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ || 3 ||
athāhaṃ vācikaṃ yajñaṃ vakṣyāmi śraddhayā saha |
parātparatarāttasmācchivāccaitanyalakṣaṇāva || 1 ||
svaśaktisahitādeva dvijā jyotirmayaḥ paraḥ ||
śabdaḥ sūkṣmaḥ svabhāvena prādurāsīdakhaṇḍitaḥ || 2 ||
sa śabdaḥ punarādhāre prāṇināmāstikottamāḥ ||
piṇḍībhūtatayā''bhāti taptajāmbūnadaprabhaḥ || 3 ||
sa punarbrahmanāyā tu praviśya hṛdayāmbujam ||
vibhaktaḥ sūkṣmarūpeṇa bhāti vahnipremaḥ svataḥ || 4 ||
brahmarandhaṃ punaḥ sākṣācchivasya sthānamuttamam ||
piṇḍībhūtatayā prāpya prakāśānandalakṣaṇe || 5 ||
tatra saṃnihite śaṃbho viśrāntiṃ labhate svataḥ ||
ādhāre paraśaktestu sthāne śabdaḥ prakāśitaḥ || 6 ||
paramekākṣaraṃ sākṣādbhavatyatyantaśobhanam ||
ājñāsaṃjñānmahāsthānādūrdhvaṃ yatsthānamuttamam || 7 ||
tatrastho'yaṃ dvijāḥ śabdaḥ sūkṣmekākṣaratāmiyāt ||
tṛtīye paramādhāre pūrake puṇyabhājane ||
ekākāratvamāproti svabhāvenākṣaradvayam || 8 ||
ayamādyaḥ paro mantraḥ suprasiddhaḥ svabhāvataḥ ||
mananatrāṇarūpatvānmantra ityabhiśabditaḥ || 9 ||
mātṛkā paramā devī mantramātā maheśvarī ||
asmādādyānmahāmantrādāvirbhūtā svabhāvataḥ || 10 ||
adhomukhī bhavedekā ekā ūrdhvamukhī bhavet ||
tasmācchrīmātṛkā śṛddhā cāṃ''dyamantrātmikī bhavet || 11||
jayamādyaḥ paro mantraḥ suprasiddhaḥ svabhāvataḥ ||
mananatrāṇarūpatvānmantra ityabhiśabditaḥ || 9 ||
mātṛkā paramā devī mantramātā maheśvarī ||
asmādādyānmahāmantrādāvirbhūtā svabhāvataḥ || 10 ||
adhomukhī bhavedekā ekā ūrdhvamukhī bhavet ||
tasmācchrī mātṛkā śuddhā cā~''dyamantrātmikī bhavet || 11||
ādyo'yaṃ paramo mantraḥ suprasiddho'pi suvratāḥ ||
gurūpadeśato jñeyo nānyathā śāstrakoṭibhiḥ || 12 ||
svaprakāśasvarūpasya vācako'yaṃ paro manuḥ ||
nāstyataḥ paramo mantro na samaśvāsya suvratāḥ ||
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyamuddhṛtya bhujamucyate || 14 ||
tricaturvatsaraṃ śiṣyaṃ parīkṣya satataṃ punaḥ ||
īśvarādeśato deyo mantro'yaṃ mantrisattamaiḥ || 15 ||
aparīkṣya pradānena śīghraṃ mṛtyumavāpnuyāt ||
jarjitaḥ puruṣārtho'pi vṛthā bhavati tasya tu || 16 ||
asya mantrasya vaiśiṣṭayaṃ mayā vaktuṃ na śakyate ||
munibhiśva tathā devaiḥ sarvajñena śivena ca || 17 ||
mantrāṇāṃ mātṛbhūtā ca mātṛkā parameśvarī || 18 ||
buddhisthā madhyamā bhūtvā vibhaktā bahudhā bhavet ||
sā punaḥ kramabhedena mahāmantrātmanā tathā || 19 ||
mantrātmanā ca vedādiśabdākāreṇa ca svataḥ ||
satyetareṇa śabdenāpyāvirbhavati suvratāḥ || 20 ||
yathā parataraḥ śaṃbhurvidhā śaktiśivātmanā ||
tathaiva mātṛkā devī dvidhābhūtā bhavetsvayam || 21 ||
ekākāreṇa śaktestu vācakaśvetareṇa tu ||
śivasya vācakaḥ sākṣādvidheyaṃ padagāminī || 22 ||
apadaṃ padamāpanaṃ padaṃ cāpyapadaṃ bhavet ||
padāpadavibhāṃgaṃ ca yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati || 23 ||
padasthasya jitā mantrā bhaveyuḥ paṇḍitottamāḥ ||
padābhyāsaparāṇāṃ tu na kiṃcidapi durlabham || 24 ||
aṃśa ekaḥ padasyāyamupakārāya dehinām ||
bhavetpoḍaśacā pūrva pañcadhā ca dvidhā punaḥ || 25 ||
padasyāṃśo'paraḥ pūrvo dvātriṃśadamāpnuyāt ||
trayastriṃśatpunarbhedaṃ tathaiva dvividhaṃ bhavet || 26 ||
evaṃ lokopakārāya padaṃ bahuvidhaṃ bhavet || 27 ||
ekaikākāra ke kāryasiddhirbhavetsvataḥ ||
vaidikānkecanā''kārānupajīvanti siddhaye || 28 ||
tāntrikāṃśca tathā''kārānupajīvanti kecana ||
laukikānapi cā''kārānupajīvanti kecana || 29 ||
yathā sarve mahādevamupajīvanti sarvadā ||
yathā vā śaktimīśasya yathā vā bhūtapañcakam ||
tathā sarve padākārānupajīvanti sarvadā || 30 ||
mātṛkā paramā devī svapadākārameditā ||
vaikharīrūpatāmeti karaṇairviśadā svayam || 31 ||
sthūlā sūkṣmā susūkṣmā ca trividhā mātṛkeśvarī ||
sā devī śaktisaṃbhinnā śivasyāmitatejasaḥ || 32 ||
vācāmagocarākāro mātṛkāyāstathā paraḥ || 33 ||
brahmaviṣṇvādidevānāmacintyaḥ sūkṣmatāvidhiḥ ||
cinmayaḥ paracidrūpaḥ śivāsaṃbhinna eva hi || 34 ||
buddhvā mantrajapaṃ kuryādevaṃ mantrasya vaibhavam ||
ācāryamukhataḥ prāṃjñāḥ sidhyatyevācireṇa tu ||
ācāryarahito mantraḥ puṃso'narthasya kāraṇam || 35 ||
iti śrīskandapurāṇe sutasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava-
caturtho'dhyāyaḥ || 4 ||
nāma caturtho'dhyāyaḥ || 4 ||
atha pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ
praṇavaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi samāsena na vistarāva ||
parāparavibhāgena praṇavastu dvidhā mataḥ || 1 ||
paraḥ parataraṃ brahma prajñānandādilakṣaṇam ||
prakarṣeṇa navaṃ yasmātparaṃ brahma svabhāvataḥ || 2 ||
aparaḥ praṇavaḥ sākṣācchabdarūpaḥ sunirmalaḥ ||
prakarṣeṇa navatvasya hetutvātpraṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ ||
paramapraṇava prāptihetutvātpraṇavo'tha vā || 3 ||
purā prajāpatiḥ sākṣācchraddhayā parayā saha || 4 ||
bhasmoddhūlitasarvāṅgastripuṇḍrāṅkitamastakaḥ ||
jitendriyo jitakrodho jaṭāvalkalasaṃyutaḥ || 5 ||
sadā pañcāgnimadhyasthaḥ sāmbadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ||
tatāpa paramaṃ ghoraṃ tapaḥ saṃvatsaratrayam || 6 ||
sa punaḥ śaṃkarasyāsya prasādādamvikāpateḥ ||
pṛthivīmantarikṣaṃ ca divaṃ cāsṛjadāstikāḥ || 7 ||
sa tānabhyatapallokāṃstebhyo vedavidāṃ varāḥ ||
trīṇi jyotīṃṣyajāyanta pṛthivyā eva tatra tu || 8 ||
ajāyatāgnirvāyuśca brāhmaṇāśvānterikṣataḥ ||
divo divākaraḥ sākṣājagaccakṣurajāyata || 9 ||
tāni cābhyatapajyotīṃṣyajastebhyo mahādvijāḥ ||
trayo vedā ajāyanta vedānāṃ prathamo'nalāva || 10 ||
yajurvedastathā vāyorādityātsāmasaṃjñitaḥ ||
vedānabhyatapattāṃśca brahmā tebhyo mahādijāḥ || 11 ||
trīṇi śuklānyajāyanta tatra brahmavidāṃ varāḥ ||
ṛgvedādeva bhūstaddadyajurvedādbhuvastathā || 12 ||
sāmavedātsuvastāni śulānyabhyatapatprabhuḥ ||
tathā tebhyo'bhitaptebhyastrayo varṇā dvijottamāḥ || 13 ||
ajāyanta krameṇaiva koṭisūryasamaprabhāḥ ||
akāraśca tathokāro makāraśceti suvratāḥ || 14 ||
tānekadhā samaradaja omityatiprabhuḥ ||
tasminneva śivaḥ sāmbaḥ sarvavastvavabhāsakaḥ ||
prativimbitavāṃstena praṇavastasya vācakaḥ || 15 ||
taptalohādivacchaṃbhorabhedātpraṇavo'pi saḥ ||
sarvāvabhāsako nityamabhavatpaṇḍitottamāḥ || 16 ||
jñātārthe jñātamityevaṃ vaktavye sati tahinā ||
omiti prāha loko'yaṃ tena jñātasya vācakaḥ ||17||
ajñātārthe tathā'jñātamiti prāpte tu vācake ||
omiti prāha loko'yaṃ tenājñātasya vācakaḥ ||18||
saṃdigdhārthe tu saṃdigdhamiti prāpte tu vācake ||
omiti prāha loko'yaṃ tena saṃdigdhavācakaḥ ||19||
ākāśādipadārthānāṃ ye śabdā vācakā bhuvi ||
vinā tānakhilā śabdāloka omiti bhāṣate ||20||
ataḥ prayogavāhulyāṭakuyyādiśabdavat ||
ākāśādipadārthānāṃ vācakaḥ praṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ || 21 ||
sarvāvabhāsakatvena brahmaṇā sadṛśaḥ smṛtaḥ || 22 ||
sarvāvabhāsakaṃ mantramimaṃ japati yo dvijaḥ ||
sarvamantrajapasyoktaṃ phalaṃ sa labhate'cirāt ||
ataḥ sarve parityajya sadā mantramimaṃ japet || 23 ||
paramātmābhivaḥ śaṃbhurdevatā parikīrtitā || 24 ||
akāro bindusaṃyuktaḥ śaktirasya dvijottamāḥ || 25 ||
ukāraśca makāraśca dvayaṃ bījaṃ prakīrtitam ||
mokṣārthe viniyogo'sya prokto vedāntavedibhiḥ ||26||
agniśva vāyuḥ sūryaśva varṇānāṃ munayaḥ kramāt ||
gāyatrī ca tathā triṣṭubbṛhatī ca yathākramam || 27 ||
chandāṃsi brahmavicchreṣṭhā varṇānāṃ ca yathākramam ||
brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśva varṇānāṃ devatāḥ kramāt || 28 ||
raktaṃ śuktaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca kramāddarṇā udāhṛtāḥ ||
jāgratsvamasuṣuptiśvāvasthāḥ proktā yathākramam || 29 ||
bhūmyantarikṣasvargāśca sthānāni kramaśo viduḥ ||
udāttapramukhā viprāḥ svarāḥ proktā manīpibhiḥ ||
ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃjñāśca vedāḥ proktā yathākramam || 30 ||
agnayo gārhapatyāgnidakṣiṇāgnistathaiva ca ||
proktaścā''havanīyāgnirvarṇānāṃ kramaśo dvijāḥ ||31||
prātarmadhyaṃdinaṃ sāyaṃ kālā uktā yathākramam ||
rajaḥ sattvaṃ tamaścaiva guṇā uktā yathākramam || 32 ||
sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśva saṃhāraḥ kriyāḥ proktā yathākramam ||
utpattau ca sthitau nāśe viniyogā udāhṛtāḥ || 33 ||
aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntamaṅgulīnāṃ ca saṃdhiṣu ||
kramādvarṇatrayanyāsaḥ kartavyaḥ siddhimicchatā || 34 ||
aṅgulīṣu ca sarvāsu praṇavanyāsa īritaḥ || 35 ||
vinyastavyāśca siddhayarthamaṅgulīṣu dvijanmanā || 36 ||
kramāddarṇatrayanyāso nābhau hṛdi ca mūrdhani ||
kartavyaḥ sarvayatnena praṇavena tathaiva ca || 37 ||
hṛdayādipradeśeṣu krameṇaiva dvijottamāḥ ||
evaṃ nyasya vidhānena dhyātvā sāmbaṃ triyambakam ||
japenmantravaraṃ bhaktyā lakṣāṇāṃ daśakaṃ dvijāḥ || 39 ||
tataḥ sidhyati mantro'yaṃ satyameva na saṃśayaḥ ||
ṣaṭkarmāṇi prasidhyanti tathaivāṣṭa vibhūtayaḥ || 40 ||
apavargaḥ svataḥsiddhaḥ pāpaiḥ sarvaiḥ pramucyate ||
sarvavidyālayo bhūtvā yatheṣṭaṃ phalamāpnuyāt || 41 ||
vicāro nāma pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ || 5 ||
nāma pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ || 5 ||
sāvitrīmatha vakṣyāmi vyāhṛtyā śirasā saha ||
bhūrādivyāhṛtīnāṃ tu munayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ || 1 ||
atrirbhṛguśva kutsaśca vasiṣṭho gautamastathā ||
kaśyapaśvāṅgirāśveti krameṇa munipuṅgavāḥ || 2 ||
vyāhṛtīnāṃ krameṇaiva chandāṃsi kathitāni tu ||
devīgāyatramādyaṃ syāduṣṇihā tadanantaram || 3 ||
anuṣṭubbṛhatī paṅaktistriṣṭup ca jagatī tathā ||
agnirvāyustathā'rkaśva vāgīśo varuṇastathā || 4 ||
indraśva viśvedevāśca krameṇaiva tu devatāḥ ||
vyāhṛtīnāṃ tu sarvatra viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || 5 ||
viśvāmitro muniśchando gāyatraṃ devatā raviḥ ||
sāvitryā vedavicchreṣṭhāḥ śiva evādhidevatā || 6 ||
tripadā sā tu sāvitrī ṣaḍbhirvarṇaiścatuṣpadā ||
jape sā tripadā jñeyā pūjāyāṃ sā catuṣpadā || 7 ||
omāpo jyotirityetadrāyatryāḥ śira uttamam ||
ṛṣirbrahmā'sya mantrasya cchando'nuṣṭup prakīrtitaḥ || 8 ||
devatā paramātmaiva proko vedārthavedibhiḥ ||
yatheṣṭasādhane cāsya viniyoga udāhṛtaḥ || 9 ||
sāvitrī tripadā jñeyā paṭṭūkṣiḥ pañcaśīrṣakā ||
agnivarṇamukhā śuklā puṇḍarīkadalekṣaṇā || 10 ||
ṛgyajuḥsāmarūpāśca pādā asyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||
pūrvā dikprathamā kukṣirdvitīyā dakṣiṇā matā || 11 ||
paścimā diktṛtīyā ca caturthī cottarā matā ||
ūrdhvā dikpañcamī kukṣiḥ ṣaṣṭhayadho dikprakīrtitā || 12 ||
aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni nābhirasyā munīśvarāḥ ||
jagaccharīraṃ sāvitryā jākāśamudarāntaram || 13 ||
stanau chandāṃsi hṛdayaṃ dharmaśāstramakalmaṣam ||
bāhavo nyāyaśāstraṃ tu karṇau sāṃkhyadayaṃ tathā || 14 ||
śikṣādyaṅgāni śīrṣāṇi vaktramagnirmahādyutiḥ ||
mīmāṃsā lakṣaṇaṃ tasyāśveśa cā''tharvaṇī śrutiḥ ||15||
brahmā mūrdhā śikhā rudro viṣṇurātmā prakīrtitaḥ ||
tasyāḥ sūkṣmaśarīraṃ ca śāstraṃ vedāntasaṃjñitam || 16 ||
antaryāmī śivaḥ sākṣātsāmbaścandrārdhaśekharaḥ ||
svaśarīre tu sāvitrīṃ vinyasedakṣarakramāt || 17 ||
pādāṅguṣṭhe tu gulphe tu jaṅghe jānupradeśake ||
ūrudeśe ca guhye ca vṛṣaṇe ca tathaiva ca || 18 ||
kaṭipradeśe nābhau ca jaṭhare stanayorhṛdi ||
kaṇṭhe ca vadane tālau nāsikāyāṃ ca cakṣupoḥ || 19 ||
bhruvormadhye lalāṭe ca pūrvavaktre tathaiva ca ||
dakṣiṇa paścime caiva tathaiva brāhmaṇottamāḥ ||
uttare ca tathā mūrdhni nyāsaḥ samyakprakīrtitaḥ || 20 ||
prathamaśvampakākāro dvitīyaḥ śyāma eva hi ||
tṛtīyaḥ piṅgalaḥ moktaścaturtho munisattamāḥ || 21 ||
indranīlasamaprakhyaḥ pañcamaḥ pāvakaprabhaḥ ||
paṣṭo vahnimabhastaddatsaptamaścāgnivarṇakaḥ || 22 ||
vidyuddarṇanibhaḥ sākṣādaṣṭamaḥ paribhāṣitaḥ ||
navamastārakāvarṇo daśamaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇakaḥ || 23 ||
tatparo raktagaurābhaḥ śyāmastatparamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||
śuklavarṇaḥ pītavarṇo raktavarṇaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ || 24 ||
śuklavarṇaḥ paro varṇaḥ padmarāgaprabhaḥ paraḥ || 25 ||
tatparaḥ śaśisaṃkāśaḥ pāṇḍuraḥ paramo mataḥ ||
tatparo ratnagaurābha indranīlasamo'tha vā || 26 ||
goraktasadṛśaśvānyastatparaḥ sūryasaṃnibhaḥ ||
nīlotpaladalaprakhyo varṇastatparamastathā || 27 ||
śaṅkhakundenduvarṇābhaḥ sākṣāddarṇaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ ||
tatparo dīpasaṃkāśaḥ kramādvarṇāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || 28 ||
keciddarṇāstu sāvitryā mahāpātakanāśanāḥ ||
upapātakapāpānāṃ varṇāḥ kecana bādhakāḥ ||
kecana kṣudrapāpānāṃ nāśakāḥ syurna saṃśayaḥ || 29 ||
nānatoyasamaṃ dānaṃ na cāhiṃsāparaṃ tapaḥ ||
na sāvitrīsamaṃ japyaṃ na vyāhṛtisamaṃ hutam ||30||
yo no'smākaṃ dhiyaścittānyantaryāmisvarūpataḥ ||
pracodayātprerayecca tasya devasya suvratāḥ || 31 ||
savituḥ svātmabhūtaṃ tu vareṇyaṃ sarvajantubhiḥ ||
bhajanīyaṃ dvijā bhargastejaścaitanyalakṣaṇam ||
tacchabdavācyaṃ sarvajñaṃ jagatsargādikāraṇam || 33 ||
svamāyāśaktisaṃbhinnaṃ śivarudrādisaṃjñitam ||
nīlagrīvaṃ virūpākṣaṃ sāmvamūrtyapalakṣitam || 34 ||
ādityadevatāyāstu prerakaṃ parameśvaram || || 35 ||
ādityenāparijñātaṃ vayaṃ dhīmahyupāsmahe ||
sāvitryāḥ kathito hyarthaḥ saṃgraheṇa mayā''dāt || 36 ||
evamarthaṃ gurorlabdhvā dattvā tasmai ca dakṣiṇām ||
caturviṃśatikaṃ lakṣaṃ japedavyagrataḥ sudhīḥ || 37 ||
mahāpātakayukto'pi siddhamantro bhavedvijaḥ ||
ājyena juhuyānmantrī sahasrāṇāṃ catuṣṭayam || 38 ||
viniyogānathānena mantreṇaiva prasādhayet ||
srātvā prātarjapennityaṃ sahasraṃ śraddhayā saha || 39 ||
apekṣitārtha sakalaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||
hutvā tu khādiraṃ samyagvṛtāktaṃ havyavāhane || 40 ||
rāhugraste rakhau viprā labhate dhanamuttamam ||
rāhusūryasamāvāye tarpayedbhāskaraṃ jalaiḥ || 41 ||
sarvakāmasamṛddhiḥ syānnātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||
karīpacūrṇato hutvā sarpipā saha mānavaḥ || 42 ||
gavāṃ goṣṭhe sahasraṃ tu bahukṣirāṃ labheta gām ||
śālyāstaṇḍulahomena kanyāsiddhirbhaviṣyati || 43 ||
śolībījasya homena prajāmiṣṭāmavāpnuyāt ||
sāvitryā jalamādāya jatvā cāṣṭasahasrakam || 44 ||
abhiṣekaṃ dvijaḥ kuryādduḥsvaprādinivṛttaye ||
śrīharī japeearttyuvināśane || 45 ||
ghṛtāhāro japeddidyāṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||
nābhimātre jale sthitvā japellakṣaṃ samāhitaḥ || 46 ||
akaṇṭakaṃ mahārājyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||
palāśapuṣpahomena mahatīṃ śriyamaśnute || 47 ||
vetasairjayādau dṛṣṭiṃ śīghramavāpnuyāt ||
madhuhomena viprendrā rājānaṃ vaśamāyāt || 48 ||
pāyasaṃ madhunā hutvā strīvaśyaṃ labhate'cirāt ||
kevalaṃ ghṛtahomena sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt || 49 ||
annasya homataśvānnaṃ prāpnuyādacireṇa tu ||
pañcagavyāśano lakṣaṃ japtvā jātismaro bhavet || 50 ||
jānumātre jale sthitvā japetpratyarthidiṅmukhaḥ ||
yuddhe vijayamāproti sahasraṃ krodhasaṃyutaḥ || 51 ||
arkasya samidho hutvā tīkṣṇatailena sādaram ||
saptāhānmārayecchamṛte vipraṃ na saṃśayaḥ || 52 ||
śatroḥ pratikṛtiṃ bhūmāvālikhyā''khyāṃ ca tahṛdi ||
saṃmākramya tu pādaina japecchaṃ rvinaśyati || 53 ||
sāvitrī pratilomā syādabhicāreṣu karmasu ||
māraṇe varṇaśaḥ śatrorbrahmāstraṃ pratilomataḥ || 54 ||
guruprasādato jñeyamanarthakaramanyathā ||
śāntaye juhuyādanau ghṛtena payasā'pi vā ||
pañcagavyena vā hutvā tilairvā śāntimāpnuyāt ||55||
āmraparṇasya homena sarvajvaravināśanam ||
udumbarabhavāśvatthaigegajāśvāmayakṣayaḥ || 56 ||
payasā''jyena vā hutvā śāntiḥ sarvacatuṣpadām ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava-

nāma ṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ || 6 ||
ātmamantraṃ pravakṣyāmi samāsena na vistarāva ||
ṛṣirbrahmā'sya gāyatraṃ chanda ātmaiva devatā ||
śāntāntaṃ śaktirasyoktā tadantaṃ bījamucyate || 1 ||
vidyā śaktirbhavedvījaṃ śiva eva na cānyathā ||
tenāyaṃ paramo mantraḥ śivaśaktyātmakaḥ smṛtaḥ || 2 ||
etadbuddhvā japenmantraṃ bījaśakyātmanā budhaḥ ||
dhyāyetsāmyaṃ mahādevaṃ saṃsārāmayabheṣajam || 3 ||
yastu dvādaśasāhasramimaṃ japati nityaśaḥ ||
tasya sarvāṇi pāpāni vinaśyanti na saṃśayaḥ || 4 ||
athavā prāṇasaṃcāraḥ sakāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||
hakāro'pānasaṃcāro dehe dehabhṛtāṃ sadā || 5 ||
evaṃ yastu vijānāti mantramācāryapūrvakam ||
so'japannapi haṃsākhyaṃ japatyeva na saṃśayaḥ || 6 ||

yo vijānāti pāpāni buddhipūrvakṛtāni ca ||
tasya naśyanti sarvāṇi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 8 ||
athavo jīvamantro'yaṃ jīvātmapratipādakaḥ ||
ahaṃśabdasya rūḍhatvāloke jīvātmavastuni ||

prakṛtārthe prasiddhatvātprasiddhaḥ parameśvaraḥ || 10 ||
mahadādyaṇuparyantaṃ jagatsarva carācaram ||
jāyate vartate caiva līyate parameśvare || 11 ||
saṃsāritvena bhāto'haṃ sa eva parameśvaraḥ ||
so'hameva na saṃdehaḥ svānubhūtipramāṇataḥ || 12 ||
haṃsayoḥ śabalaṃ hitvā padayoḥ sadditīyayoḥ ||
pūrṇo'hamevaṃ jānīyādbodhamātrasvabhāvataḥ || 13 ||
śrutirapyevamevā''ha paramārthaprakāśinī ||

ahaṃ cāvyabhicāritvātsatsvabhāvo na saṃśayaḥ ||
ahamavyabhicāryeva sākṣitvādvyabhicāriṇām || 15 ||
jñātamajñātamapyarthaṃ sadā'haṃ veda kevalaḥ ||
so'rtho māṃ na vijānāti tato'vicchinnacetanaḥ || 16 ||
cito'nyaśepatābhāvāccito'cicchepatā na hi ||

tathā cicetanasyāpi na śeṣatvamavāpnuyāt ||

ato'nyaśeṣatā loke cito bhrāntyā pratīyate ||
sukhasvabhāva evāhaṃ sadā premāspadatvataḥ || 20 ||
asukhasya na hi premāspadatvaṃ paridṛśyate ||
nāhamanyasya śeṣo hi śeṣī sarvasya sarvadā || 21 ||
pūrṇo'haṃ sarvasākṣitvātsarvadā paramārthataḥ ||
apūrṇo yugapatsarvaṃ na vijānāti kaścana || 22 ||
saṃsāravarjitaḥ sākṣātsarvadā parameśvaraḥ ||
ahaṃ saṃsārasākṣitvāttathā saṃsāravarjitaḥ || 23 ||
evaṃ vākyānusāriṇyā yuktyā''cāryapuraḥsaram ||
ahaṃ sa so'hameveti vijānīyādvicakṣaṇaḥ || 24 ||
ya evamātmamantreṇa jīvātmaparamātmanoḥ ||
pāramārthikamekatvaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ paripaśyati ||
sa eva brahmavinmukhyo netaro'jñānamohitaḥ || 25 ||
evaṃbhūtaṃ parijñānaṃ yasya jātaṃ yadā bhuvi ||
tadaiva tasya saṃsāravināśo nāsti saṃśayaḥ || 26 ||
haṃsavidyāmavijñāya muktau yatnaṃ karoti yaḥ ||

haṃsavidyā parā caiṣā paramantraprabhedinī ||
sarvaiśvaryapradā sarvadevatā tṛptikāriṇī || 28 ||
asyāśca japamātreṇa dīrghāyuṣyamavāpnuyāt ||
ārogyaṃ vijayaṃ vidyāmavāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ || 29 ||
bahunoktena kiṃ vidyā haṃsākhyā sarvakāmadā ||
haṃsa haṃseti yo brūyātsarvadā śiva eva saḥ || 30 ||
śivena viṣṇunā caiva brahmaṇā sarvadaivataiḥ ||
jātā haṃsavidheyamacirādeva siddhidā || 21 ||
recakaṃ narakaṃ muktvā kumbhake susthitaḥ sudhīḥ ||
nābhikande samau kṛtvā prāṇāpānau samāhitaḥ || 32 ||

dīpākāraṃ mahādevaṃ jvalantaṃ nābhimadhyame || 33 ||
evaṃ dine dine kuryādaṇimādivibhūtaye ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava-

nāma saptamo'dhyāyaḥ || 7 ||
paḍakṣaraṃ pravakṣyāmi samāsena suśobhanam ||
yena saṃsāravicchittirbrahmendrādivibhūtayaḥ || 1 ||
devatā'sya śivaḥ sākṣātsatyajñānasukhādayaḥ || 2 ||
śaktirmāheśvarī sā ca bhuvaneśākṣaraṃ bhavet ||
vījaṃ māyāviśiṣṭastu śivaḥ pūrvoktalakṣaṇaḥ || 3 ||
so'pi tacchabda eva syānnyāsaḥ pañcākṣaraiḥ kramāt ||
aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ vinyasedakṣaraṃ kramāt || 4 ||
mastake ca lalāṭe ca hṛdi nābhau padadvaye ||
punaḥ pañcākṣareṇaiva pañcāṅgaṃ visanyetkramāt || 5 ||
praṇavaṃ prathamaṃ vidyādditīyaṃ tu nakārakam ||
makāraṃ tatparaṃ vidyācchikāraṃ tu tataḥ param || 6 ||
vakāraṃ pañcamaṃ vidyādyakāraṃ paṣṭhameva ca ||
itthaṃ paḍakṣaraṃ vidyājjābālopaniṣadgatam || 7||
satyajñānaparānandasvarūpasya śivasya tu || 8 ||
asaṃpṛktyā śivasyāyaṃ śivaśabdastu vācakaḥ ||
namaḥ śabdo namaskāravācakaḥ parikīrtitaḥ || 9 ||
prahṛtālakṣaṇaḥ prokto namaskāraḥ purātanaiḥ ||
prahnatā nāma jīvasya śivātsatyādilakṣaṇāt || 10 ||
bhedena bhāsamānasya māyayā na svarūpataḥ ||
saṃbandha eva tenaiva so'pi tādātmyalakṣaṇaḥ || 11 ||
nityasiddha ḥ śivaḥ sākṣātsvarūpaḥ sarvadehinām ||
tasmādubhutsorjīvasya nopādeyaṃ hitaṃ sadā || 12 ||
na heyamahitaṃ taddaddastuto na pratītitaḥ ||
evaṃ vidyānnakārārthaṃ makārārtha udīryate || 13 ||
vyāvahārikadṛṣṭyā'yaṃ namaskāraḥ prakīryate || 14

joṅkāraśabdaḥ sarvārthavācakaḥ parikīrtitaḥ || 15 ||
prayogādeva sarvatra sarvārthaḥ śiva eva hi ||
tasmācchivasya pūrṇasya praṇavo vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ ||16||
vācyavācakabhāvaśva lakṣyalakṣaṇatā'pi ca ||
anyonyatā'pi nāstyeva paramārthanirūpaṇe || 17 ||
abhāvādeva sarvasya śivādanyasya sarvadā ||
asti nāsti mṛpā bhāti na bhātītyādi māyayā || 18 ||
kalpitaṃ citsukhānantaparamātmaśivātmani ||
māyātatkāryamapyasmācchivātsatyādilakṣaṇāva ||
pratyakṣasiddhānnāstyeva paramārthanirūpaṇe || 19 ||
atha kiṃ bahunoktena śivādanyanna vidyate || 20 ||
śivasvarūpamevā''huridaṃ sarva vicakṣaṇāḥ ||
sarvasvarūpamajñānādṛśyate na tu vastutaḥ || 21 ||
epa eva hi mantrārthaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ na cānyathā ||

anyānyapi ca śāstrāṇi tathā tarkāśva sarvaśaḥ ||
śaivāgamāśca vividhā āgamā vaiṣṇavā api || 23 ||

mantrārthaḥ kathitaḥ kṛtsraḥ pauraśvaryāSdhunocyate ||

phalamūlāśano vā'pi haviṣyāśī yathāvalam ||

vane vā nirbhaye śuddhe prāṅmukhodaṅmukho'pi vā ||

karanyāsaṃ punaḥ kṛtvā tathā'ṅganyāsameva ca ||

hṛtpuṇḍarīkamadhye tu somasūryāgnimaṇḍale ||

athavā sāmvamīśānaṃ śrīsadāśivameva ca ||
nṛtyamānaṃ tathā deveṃ dhyātvā mantraṃ tu sādhayet ||35||
athavā prākṛtaṃ bhāvaṃ svīyamutsṛjya sarvadā ||
śivo'hamiti saṃcintya sādhayedidamuttamam || 36 ||

nityaṃ dvādaśasāhasraṃ japeddhatayā samāhitaḥ || 37 ||

paṣṭirlakṣajapenaiva labhate brahmaṇaḥ padam ||

paṭakarmāṇi prasidhyanti daśalakṣajapena tu ||

athavā maṇḍale saure candramaṇḍalake'thavā ||

āsanaṃ prathamaṃ dadyādāvāhanamanantaram ||
arghyaṃ tataḥ paraṃ dadyātpādyaṃ caiva tataḥ param || 44 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavaibhava-
khaṇḍe paḍakṣaravivaraṇaṃ nāmāṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ || 8||
varaṇaṃ nāmāṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ || 8 ||
dhyānayajñamathedānīṃ pravakṣyāmi samāsataḥ ||
śṛṇuta śraddhayā yūyaṃ bhuktimuktiphalapradam || 1 ||
parātparataraṃ tattvaṃ dhyeyaṃ mūtryātmanaiva tu ||
na svarūpeṇa sākṣitvādātmatvādviṣayitvataḥ || 2 ||
bhedābhāvācca bhedasya bhramatvādeva vastutaḥ ||
umārdhavigrahā śuklā candrārdhakṛtaśekharā || 3 ||
nīlagrīvā trinetrā ca prasannavadanā śubhā ||
varadābhayahastā ca vicitra mukuṭojjvalā || 4 ||
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā ||
svasvarūpānusaṃdhānapramodādeva kevalāva || 5 ||
mahātāṇḍavasaṃyuktā brahmaviṣṇuśivādibhiḥ ||
dhyeyā''dyantavinirmuktā yā mūrtiḥ śrutidarśitā || 6 ||
saivāsādhāraṇā mūrtiḥ parātparatarasya tu ||
ye sadā paramāṃ mūrti dhyāyanti hṛdayāmbuje ||
imāṃ te paramāṃ muktiṃ muktiṃ ca prāpnuvanti hi || 7 ||
jñānājñānamahāmāyālakṣaṇāvidyayā saha ||
abhedena sthitaṃ viprāḥ parātparataraṃ padam || 8 ||
svapradhānatayopāsyaṃ tathaivāsvapradhānataḥ ||
samapradhānarūpeṇāpyādareṇa manīṣibhiḥ || 9 ||
svapradhānatayā tattvamupāste śuddhamānasaḥ ||
tathaivāpakvacittastu paratattvaṃ dvijottamāḥ || 10 ||
asvapradhānarūpeṇa tathā martyastu madhyamaḥ ||

jāḍyākārastu yaḥ śaktestenābhinnaṃ paraṃ padam ||

tathā śaktestu yo jñānākārastenaikatāṃ gatam ||
paratattvaṃ tridhopāsyaṃ parijñānavatāṃ varāḥ || 13 ||
māyākāraikatāpannamapi tattvaṃ manīṣibhiḥ || 14 ||
upāsyaṃ trividhaṃ proktaṃ tathaivāvidyayaiva tu ||
abhedena sthitaṃ brahma tridhopāsyaṃ manīṣibhiḥ || 15 ||
anye ca śakterākārā ye vidyante vicakṣaṇāḥ ||
tairapyekatvamāpannaṃ tattvaṃ taddanmanīṣibhiḥ || 16 ||
upāsyaṃ trividhaṃ nityamatīva śraddhayā saha ||
īkṣaṇopādhisaṃpannaṃ paratattvamapi dvijāḥ ||
svapradhānādirūpeṇa tridhopāsyamatipriyāt || 17 ||
sattvaṃ rajastamaśveti guṇā ye brahmaśaktijāḥ ||
tairapyekatvamāpannaṃ paraṃ brahma yathākramam ||18|
rudraḥ prajāpatirviṣṇuriti bhedamupaiti ca || 19 ||
te jagannāśasargādeḥ kartāraḥ kāryarūpiṇaḥ ||
upāsyāstrividhā nityaṃ te'pi svaṃ svamupādhibhiḥ||20||
tairgṛhītāstathā viprā mūrtayastriprakārataḥ ||

śabdasparśādisaṃjñā ye padārthāḥ pañca te'pi ca ||
upāsyā brahmarūpeṇa mahāprājñairmanīpibhiḥ || 23 ||
ākāśādīni bhūtāni yāni tāni manīṣibhiḥ ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyāni mahātmabhiḥ || 24 ||
bhautikā aṇḍabhedāśva brahmarūpeṇa sādaram ||
cintanīyāśca vidyadbhirvedavedāntapāragāḥ || 25 ||
aṇḍamadhye sthitā lokā ete'pi brahmavittamāḥ ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyā eva sūribhiḥ || 26 ||
lokāntarvartino deśā ete'pi dijapuṅgavāḥ ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyā munisattamaiḥ || 27 ||
merumandārapūrvāśca parvatā vividhā dvijāḥ ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyā vedavittamāḥ || 28 ||
nadīnadādayaḥ sarve devarṇyādivinirmitāḥ ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyāḥ puruṣottamaiḥ || 29 ||
vāpīkūpataḍāgādyā api vedaparāyaṇāḥ ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyāḥ puruṣādhikaiḥ || 30 ||
vanāni yāni loke tu vividhāni mahattamāḥ ||
tāni brahmatayā nityamupāsyāni tapodhanaiḥ || 31 ||
samudrāśva sadā viprāḥ samudrāntargatā api ||
diśaśva vidiśaścaiva divārātraṃ tathaiva ca ||
anāgatādayaḥ kālā upāsyā brahmarūpataḥ || 33 ||
aṇḍajaṃ jārajaṃ caiva svedajaṃ codvijaṃ tathā ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyā mohavarjitaiḥ || 34 ||
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā api ca saṃkarāḥ ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyā eva sūribhiḥ || 35 ||
āśramā brahmacaryādyāstadācārā api dvijāḥ ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyāḥ paramāstikaiḥ || 36 ||
mahāpātakapūrvāṇi pāpāni subahūni ca ||
brahmarūpatayā nityamupāsyāni mahattamaiḥ || 37 ||
dharmasaṃjñāśca ye viprā uttamādhamamadhyamāḥ ||
te'pi brahmatayā nityamupāsyāḥ paṇḍitottamaiḥ ||38||
sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ tayorbhogaḥ sādhanaṃ tasya suvratāḥ ||
brahmarūpatayā sarvamupāsyaṃ satyavādibhiḥ || 39 ||
kartā kārayitā karma karaṇaṃ kāryameva ca ||
brahmarūpatayā sarvamupāsyaṃ cetanottamaiḥ || 40 ||
pramātā ca pramāṇaṃ ca prameyaṃ pramitistathā ||

sati bhede viśeṣaḥ syānnābhede hi munīśvarāḥ || 4 ||
bhedākārastu sattāyāvidyate yadi vastutaḥ ||
bhedākārastu sattāyā bhinnaśvecchūnyatattvavat ||
śūnyameva bhavennaiva bhedākāro bhaveddijāḥ || 5 ||
bhedākāraḥ sa sattāyā abhinnaścetsa saiva hi || 6 ||
bhinnābhinnau yadi syātāṃ dopahayasamāgamaḥ ||
tasmātsattātirekeṇa viśeṣārtho na vidyate || 7 ||
viśeṣārthapratītistu bhrāntisiddhā na saṃśayaḥ ||
ata ekā sadā sattā saiva brahma parātparam ||
sattāyā yadi bhinnaṃ cedbrahmāsatsyānṛśṛṅgavat || 8 ||
tatraivaṃ sati viprendrā ye padārthā ghaṭādayaḥ ||
te tu sattātirekeṇa na vidyante kathaṃcana || 9 ||
brahmaivedamiti prāha śrutirapyatinirmalā || 10 ||
viduṣāmanubhūtiśca tathaiva hi na saṃśayaḥ ||
ataḥ sarvamidaṃ śaṃbhuriti vitta vicakṣaṇāḥ || 11 ||
tathā sarvatayā bhāti śivaḥ sarvāvabhāsakaḥ ||
kaṭakādivibhedena yathā hema prakāśate ||
tathā sarvatayā bhāti śivaḥ sarvāvabhāsakaḥ || 13 ||
śaktikā rajatākārā yathā bhāti svabhāvataḥ |
tathā sarvatayā bhāti śivaḥ sarvāvabhāsakaḥ || 14 ||
svapnadṛksvamarūpeṇa yathā bhāti svabhāvataḥ ||
tathā sarvatayā bhāti śivaḥ sarvāvibhāsakaḥ || 15 ||
andhakāraḥ prakāśaśca yathā''kāśe prakāśate ||

mahadādiviśepāntaṃ jagadbhāti tathā''tmani || 17 ||

cidātmarūpaṃ vidurenameva || 21 ||
paramarūpatayaiva vibhāti hi || 22 ||
kathamaśeṣajagatpratibhā bhavet || 23 ||
hṛdayakuharamadhye saṃcitaṃ karmavṛndam |

dbrahmavedanameva taduttamam || 26 ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe sutasaṃhitāyāṃ caturthe yajñavebhavakhaṇḍe

vaibhavakhaṇḍe jñānaviśeṣayogo nāma pañcadaśo'dhyāyaḥ || 15 ||
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi jñānotpattestu kāraṇam ||
vinā yena śivajñānaṃ na jāyeta kathaṃcana || 1 ||
mumukṣuratisaṃtuṣṭaḥ sidhyatyeva gatirmama ||
iti niśvayabudvistu pratibandhanivṛttaye ||
devatāḥ sakalā nityaṃ prārthayenmatimattamaḥ || 2 ||
śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ no bhavatu cāryamā || 3 ||
śaṃ na indraśca vāgīśaḥ śaṃ no viṣṇururukramaḥ ||
namo'stu brahmaṇe vāyo namo'stu tava śobhanam || 4 ||
tvameva sākṣādbrahmāsi tvāṃ vadiṣyāmi śaṃkaram ||
ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ cāhaṃ tvāṃ vadiṣyāmi viśeṣataḥ || 5 ||
tanmāmavatu kalyāṇaṃ tadvaktāraṃ ca śobhanam ||
māṃ bhūyo'vatu vaktāramapi cāvatu śobhanam || 6 ||
śāntiḥ śāntiḥ punaḥ śāntirdoṣatrayanivṛttaye ||

me gopāyetiparyantamaryantaśraddhayā saha || 8 ||

upakṣīṇā bhavedvistatra tasya na saṃśayaḥ || 9 ||
ataḥ saṃkocahānāya vidyārthī tu dine dine ||

bhasmanā tena sarvānaṃ samuḍūlya tataḥ param || 22 ||

ciraṃtanāni sthānāni śivasyāmitatejasaḥ ||

śivasyotsavasevārthe gacchecchraddhāpuraḥsaram ||
utsavaṃ sevamānasya muktirhastasthitā bhavet || 25 ||
viśiṣṭamantraṃ bhuñjīta cittaśuddhyarthamātmanaḥ ||
nirmālyaṃ ca nivedyaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa vivarjayet || 26 ||

nirmālyaṃ ca nivedyaṃ ca bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ||28||

| saha pramodaṃ saṃsṛṣṭi saha paṅktau tu bhojanam ||

uktasādhanasaṃpanno jñānādbhasmādhigacchati || 37 ||

tatprasādena sarveṣāṃ devatvaṃ na svabhāvataḥ ||

bhasmasaṃchannasarvāṅgāstripuṇḍrāṅkitamastakāḥ ||

iti śrīskandapurāṇe sūtasaṃhitāyāṃ jñānotpattikāraṇa-
varṇanaṃ nāma poḍaśo'dhyāyaḥ || 16 ||
raṇaviśeṣavarṇanaṃ nāma poḍaśo'dhyāyaḥ || 16 ||
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vairāgyaṃ duḥkhanāśanam ||
yena sākṣācchivajñānaṃ jāyate mokṣasādhanam || 1 ||
pratyagbrahmakatājñānādvaita vastu samudratam ||

ājñayā devadevasya kālapākena karmaṇām ||

śobhanatvena saṃklapte viṣaye vāsanāvalāva ||
icchā nityaṃ prajāyeta narāṇāṃ mūḍhacetasām || 4||

eka aihika ākhyāta itaraḥ pāralaukikaḥ || 5 ||
aihikānindriyairarthānbhuṅkte dehī nirantaram ||

iha loke paratrāpi dveṣastatra hi jāyate || 10 ||

śukraṃ ca śoṇitaṃ dṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvā smṛtvā tu mānavaḥ ||
udvāraṃ kurute tadvi śarīraṃ cetanasya tu || 12 ||
tasmiñśarīre'haṃnuddhiṃ sadā kaḥ kurute janaḥ ||
mūḍho'haṃ mamabuddhibhyāmidaṃ gṛhṇāti vigraham || 13 ||

tathaivā''tmatayā'grāhye śarīre carma yadbhavet ||

tathaivā''tmatayā'grāhye dehe māṃsaṃ tu yadbhavet || 17 ||

tathaivā''tmatayā'grāhyā śarīrasthā ca yā śirā ||

mūḍho'haṃmamabuddhibhyāmidaṃ gṛhṇāti saṃtatam ||
dṛṣṭvā sṣṭaṣṭvā tathā smṛtvā cāsthi bhūmitale sthitam ||21||

tathaivā''tmatayā'grāhyaṃ śarīrasyāsthi yadbhavet ||22||

mūḍho'haṃmama badvibhyāmidaṃ gṛhṇāti saṃtatam || 23 ||
dṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvā tathā smṛtvā romapuñjaṃ bhuvi sthitam ||

tathā dehasthitaṃ romanicayaṃ yadvijottamāḥ ||
tasminneva khabuddhiṃ sadā kaḥ kurute janaḥ || 25 ||
mūḍho'haṃmamabuddhibhyāmidaṃ gṛhṇāti saṃtatam ||

udgāraṃ kurute martyaḥ svayaṃ taddoṣadarśanāda ||
tathaivāSStmatayā'grāhyaṃ raktaṃ yaddehasaṃsthitam || 27 ||

kaḥ karoti tvahaṃbuddhiṃ mūḍha eva karoti hi || 37 ||

raktajāḥ krimayo'nantā māṃsajāḥ krimayastathā ||
krimikośamidaṃ varṣma duḥkhāya na sukhāya hi ||44||
garbha tu kalalāvasthaṃ kṛmibhirbhakṣitaṃ bhavet ||
duḥkhameva tadā saukhyaṃ na kiṃcidapi vidyate || 45 ||
bubudākāratāpanaṃ bhakṣayanti kalevaram ||
krimayo duḥkhameva syāttadā saukhyaṃ na kiṃcana ||46||
jaṭharāgnau bhavettaptaṃ garbhaṃ mātuḥ sadaiva tu ||
duḥkhameva tadā tasya sukhaṃ kiṃcinna vidyate || 47 ||
jaṭhare vāyusaṃcāracūrṇite garbhatāṃ gataḥ ||
duḥkhameva tadā tasya sukhaṃ kiṃcinna vidyate || 48 ||
purīṣamūtrasaṃpūrṇe jaṭhare garbhatāṃ gataḥ ||
duḥkhameva sadā yāti na kiṃcitsukhamāpnuyāt || 49 ||
jarāyumadhye niśchidre nimagno garbhatāṃ gataḥ ||
duḥkhameva sadā yāti na kiṃcitsukhamāpnuyāt ||50||
rauravādiṣu yaduḥkhaṃ narakeṣu nirantaram ||
garbhe tatkoṭiguṇitaṃ bhavedduḥkhaṃ na saṃśayaḥ || 51 ||
garbhe tu jāyamānasya duḥkhaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyate ||
maho durvāsa evāsya garbhavāso munīśvarāḥ || 52 ||
vālye pīḍā mahātītrā gaṇapīḍā mahattarā ||
pipīlikādipīḍā ca parihartuṃ na śakyate || 53 ||
vyādhipīḍā mahātītrā kṣutpīḍā ca dine dine ||
pipāsā ca mahāpīḍā kathaṃ yoti sukhaṃ naraḥ || 54 ||
akṣaragrahaṇe pīḍā pīḍā ca paṭhane tathā ||
śabdajālasya duḥkhābdherna pāro dṛśyate mayā || 55 ||
śrautasmārtasadācāre mahāpīḍā ca dāruṇā ||
niṣiddhaparihāre ca kathaṃ yāti sukhaṃ naraḥ || 56 ||
yauvane ca mahāduḥkhaṃ strīsaṃsarge mahattaram ||
strībhogātmakatā duḥkhaṃ duḥkhameva vicārataḥ || 57 ||
strīṇāmārādhane duḥkhaṃ tāsāṃ saṃrakṣaṇe'pi ca ||
tāsāṃ paribhave duḥkhaṃ duḥkhameva vicārataḥ || 58 ||
vastrasaṃpādane duḥkhaṃ bhūṣaṇānāṃ tathaiva ca ||
rakṣaṇe ca tathā teṣāṃ duḥkhameva vicārataḥ || 59 ||
gṛhakṣetra dhanādīnāṃ duḥkhaṃ saṃpādane tathā ||
rakṣaṇe ca tathā duḥkhaṃ teṣāmeva vicārataḥ || 60 ||

yajjñānena śivajñānaṃ jāyate sudṛḍhaṃ dvijāḥ || 1 ||

sāṃkhyasyotpattivelāyāṃ mocakasya śivasya tu || 13 ||
prasādo jāyate tena saṃsārasya vimardanam ||
saṃsāramocakaḥ sākṣācchiva eva na cāparaḥ || 14 ||
anyāśva devatāḥ sarvāḥ praṇāyaiva hi mocakāḥ ||
anekajanmasaṃsiddhaḥ śrautasmārtaparāyaṇaḥ || 15 ||
krameṇaiva mahādevaṃ mocakaṃ parameśvaram ||

prasādahetubhūteṣu praṇavākhyo mahāmanuḥ ||

oṃkārasya prasādena viṣṇoścaiva prasādataḥ ||
rudvārādhanavāñchā syāttadārādhanataḥ punaḥ || 19 ||
jñānamānandamadvaitaṃ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati ||

brāhmaṇyaṃ kīrtirindośva kherārogyameva tu || 21 ||
agnereśvaryamatulaṃ pitṛyāṇo yamasya tu ||

vighnarājasya devasya kāryasiddhiravinataḥ ||
paṇmukhasya prasādena sarvasiddhirayatnataḥ || 23 ||
bhāratyāśva prasādena vāgvibhūtirayatnataḥ ||
śrīdevyāstu prasādena sarvaiśvaryamayatnataḥ || 24 ||
durgādevyāḥ prasādena sarvatra vijayo bhavet ||
kāmināṃ devatāḥ sarvāḥ sāṃsārikaphalapradāḥ || 25 ||
kāmanārahitānāṃ tu śuddhidvāreṇa devatāḥ ||
mahādevaprasādasya hetubhūtā bhavanti hi || 26 ||
mahādevaprasādastu na hetuḥ kasyacidvijāḥ ||
svayaṃ muktikaraḥ puṃsāṃ kāmināmacireṇa tu || 27 ||
svayaṃ muktikaraḥ sākṣātkāmanārahitasya tuṃ ||
cireṇaiva tu kālena śivasyaiva prasādataḥ || 28 ||
devatā muktidā eva muktidā na svatantrataḥ ||
mahādevaprasādena samaḥ kaśvinna vidyate || 29 ||
mahādevaprasādena khalu viṣṇupadaṃ dvijāḥ ||
brahmendrādipadaṃ cāpi na svataḥ sarvadehinām || 30 ||
prasāde sati devasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ ||
vaidikānāṃ tathā'nyeṣāmapi muktirhi sidhyati || 31 ||
brāhmaṇāśca vimucyante prasādena śivasya tu ||
kṣatriyāśva tathā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā api ca saṃkarāḥ ||32||
pāpaṇḍino vimucyante prasādena śivasya tu ||
kiṃ punarvaidikā viprāḥ striyaḥ sarvā munīśvarāḥ || 33 ||
kharoṣṭrataravo'pīśaprasādenaiva kevalam ||
jayatnena vimucyante nātra saṃdehakāraṇam || 34 ||
garbhastho mucyate kaśvijjātamātreṇa kaścana ||
bālyayauvanavārdhakyādyavasthāsu ca kaścana || 35 ||
pāpaṇḍāśca vimucyante prasādena maheśituḥ ||
vaidikāśva kharoṣṭrādijātayaśca tathaiva ca || 36 ||
pāṃsavaḥ parvatāyante pāṃsūyante ca parvatāḥ ||
śivaprasādayuktānāmājñayaiva tu kevalam || 37 ||
brahmanārāyaṇādyāstu devatā akhilā api ||
vijāyante ca naśyanti hyājñayaiva prasādinaḥ || 38 ||
prasādasya ca māhātmyaṃ śivasya paramātmanaḥ ||
api devā na jānanti śrutayaśva na saṃśayaḥ || 39 ||
śaṃkaro'pi mahātejāḥ śāṃkarī vā munīśvarāḥ ||
śivaprasādamāhātmyaṃ kiṃtu jānāti vā na vā ||40||
bhavanto'pi mahādevaprasādāya munīśvarāḥ ||
gurupādāmbujaṃ nityaṃ pūjayadhvaṃ yathāvalam || 41 ||
śrīmānapure puṇye sarvadevasamānṛte ||
svasvarūpānusaṃdhānapramodeneva kevalam || 42 ||
sākṣāda sabhāmadhye nṛtyantaṃ devanāyakam ||
ambikāsahitaṃ nityaṃ bhajadhvaṃ parayā mudā || 43 ||
śrīkālahastināthasya praṇāmālokanādayaḥ ||
api śaṃbhoḥ prasādāya bhavanti dvijapuṅgavāḥ || 44 ||
vārāṇasyāṃ mahādevapraṇāmālokanādayaḥ ||
api śaṃbhoḥ prasādāya bhavanti dvijapuṅgavāḥ || 45 ||
tathāvidhaprasādalābhāya tatsādhanamupadiśati bhavanto'pītyādinā || 41 ||
prasādalābhāya hi sarvamīritam || 46 ||
śivaprasādena hi sarvamāstikāḥ || 47 ||
śivaprasādena viśuddhatā''tmanaḥ || 48 ||

prasādakamavarṇanaṃ nāma trayoviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 23 ||
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi prasādasya tu vaibhavam ||
atyantaśraddhayopetāḥ śṛṇutātīva śobhanam || 1 ||
purā kaścinmahāpāpī durghaṭo nāma nāmataḥ ||
jātyā śūdro mehākruddho mahāsāhasikottamaḥ || 2 ||
abhūttena mahāmohādvāhmaṇānāṃ śataṃ hatam ||
gavāṃ śataṃ hataṃ tena dagdhaṃ gehaśataṃ tathā || 3 ||
atha caurya kṛtaṃ tena narāṇāmavicārataḥ ||
balātparastriyo muktā bahuśo dṛṣṭigocarāḥ || 4 ||
vāpīkūpataḍāgādijalaṃ tenaiva dūṣitam ||
varṇāśramasaṃmācāramaryādā tena bheditā || 5 ||
sahasrajanmataḥ pūrve durghaṭena munīśvarāḥ ||
śivayogikare tena suvarṇa niṣkamuttamam || 6 ||
dattaṃ tena matistasya jātā kālena śobhanā ||
aho mohena pāpāni kṛtāni subahūni ca || 7 ||
mayā teṣāṃ na paśyāmi vināśasya tu kāraṇam ||
brāhmaṇā vedavidvāṃso vadanti narakānmama || 8 ||
iti vyākulacittasya durghaṭasya durātmanaḥ ||
matipradānaṃ kṛtavānbrāhmaṇaḥ kaśvidostikaḥ || 9 ||
śrīmadyāghrapuraṃ nāma sthānamasti mahītale |
yatra nṛtyati viśvātmā śivaḥ saṃsāramocakaḥ || 10||
yasya māhātmyavijñānādviṣṇurviśvajaganmayaḥ ||
tatāpa paramaṃ ghoraṃ tapastatreśvaraṃ prati || 11 ||
yasya māhātmyavijñānādvahmā viśvāmarādhipaḥ ||
tatāpa paramaṃ ghoraṃ tapastatreśvaraṃ prati || 12 ||
yasya māhātmyavijñānādindraḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ||
tatāpa paramaṃ ghoraṃ tapastatreśvaraṃ prati || 13 ||
yasya māhātmyavijñānāddevā yakṣāśva kiṃnarāḥ ||
taptavanto mahāghoraṃ tapastatreśvaraṃ prati || 14 ||
yasya māhātmyavijñānānmunayo munisattamāḥ ||
taptavanto mahāghoraṃ tapastatreśvaraṃ prati || 15 ||
yatra sarveśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā prasādaṃ labdhavānhariḥ ||
tatra devamupāssva tvaṃ pranṛtyantamumāpatim || 16 ||
yatra sarveśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā prasādaṃ labdhavānajaḥ ||
tatra devamupāssva tvaṃ pranṛtyantamumāpatim || 17 ||
yatra vajrī haraṃ dṛṣṭvā prasādaṃ labdhavāndijāḥ ||
tatra devamupāssva tvaṃ pranṛtyantamumāpatim || 18 ||
yatra dṛṣṭvā haraṃ devā aśeṣā āstikottamāḥ ||
yakṣarākṣasagandharvasiddhavidyādharādayaḥ || 19 ||
prasādaṃ labdhavantastu svādhikārānurūpataḥ ||
tatra devamupāssva tvaṃ pranṛtyantamumāpatim || 20 ||
ityevaṃ brāhmaṇenoko durghaṭaḥ puṇyagauravāda ||
śrīmadvyāghrapuraṃ gatvā śraddhayā parayā saha || 21 ||
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā jñātvā nityamatandritaḥ ||
namontaṃ śivamantraṃ tu japitvā'ṣṭottaraṃ śatam || 22 ||
śrīmadabhrasabhāmadhye pranṛtyantamumāpatim ||

vatsarāṇāṃ tryaṃ tatra uvāsātipriyeṇa saḥ || 25 ||

bhūyo'pi devadevasya prasādasya tu vaibhavam ||
pravakṣyāmi samāsena śṛṇuta śraddhayā saha || 1 ||
purā kaśvidvijaśreṣṭhaḥ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutaḥ ||
satyasaṃdhābhidhaḥ śuddho viṣṇubhakto viśeṣataḥ || 2 ||
abhūttena kṛtaṃ sarva śrutismṛtyuditaṃ mudā ||
pratiṣṭhā ca kṛtā viṣṇorvahuśaḥ paṇḍitottamāḥ || 3 ||
ārādhitaśca bhagavānviṣṇurviśvajaganmayaḥ ||
dine dine mahābhaktyā sugandhakusumādibhiḥ || 4 ||
vaiṣṇavā vividhā mantrāstena japtā dine dine ||
ciraṃtanāni sthānāni viṣṇordṛṣṭāni sādaram || 5 ||
vaiṣṇavā manujāstena pūjitāśca dine dine ||
sarvasvaṃ vaiṣṇave dattaṃ satyasaṃdhena sādaram || 6 ||
punarnārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ||
pratyakṣamabhavattasya prasannaḥ paṅkajekṣaṇaḥ || 7 ||
taṃ dṛṣṭvā satyasaṃdhastu prasanendriyamānasaḥ ||
praṇamya daṇḍavadbhūmau bhaktyā paramayā saha || 8 ||
gandhapuṣpādibhirdivyaiḥ samārādhya yathābalam ||
stotumārabhate viṣṇuṃ viśvalokaikakāraṇam || 9 ||
viṣṇave viśvalokānāṃ hetave vividhātmane ||
vedavedāntaniṣṭhānāmātmabhūtāya te namaḥ || 10 ||
kṛṣṇāya śahantre ca mama kenāpi hetunā ||
pratyakṣāya prabodhāya viduṣāmātmane namaḥ || 11||
keśavāyātiśudvāya kevalāya parātmane ||
keṣāṃcicchuddhacittānāṃ prasannāya namo namaḥ || 12 ||
muñjakeśāya muṇḍāya muṇḍināmārtihāriṇe ||
maunaniṣṭhasya mūrkhasya muktidāya namo namaḥ || 13 ||
śrīvatsāṅkāya varyāya varadāya parātmane ||
vañcakānāmagamyāya vastubhūtoya te namaḥ || 14 ||
pītavāsāya pītāya pāpapañjarahāriṇe ||
pāpakarmaparāṇāṃ tu bhañjakāya namo namaḥ || 16 ||
viṣvaksenāya viśvāya viśvotpatyādihetave ||
viśvavijñānarūpāya nirmalāya namo namaḥ || 17 ||
viśvarūpāya viśvāsalabhyāyāviditātmane ||
viśvottīrṇāya viśvasya sākṣirūpāya te namaḥ || 18 ||
murāriṇe muhūrtāya muhūrtasya vidhāyine ||
muhūrta bhajatāṃ nṛṇāṃ muktidāya namo namaḥ || 19 ||
śauriṇe śārṅgiṇe tubhyaṃ śaṃkhakundendurūpiṇe |
śākamūlaparāṇāṃ tu śāntidāya namo namaḥ || 20 ||
mukundāya mukundasya mahāmūrkhasya rakṣasaḥ ||
hartre bhatre viśiṣṭānāmātmane viduṣāṃ namaḥ || 22 ||
govindāya gavāṃ nityaṃ pālakāya parātmane ||
nandagopāya guptāya namaḥ sarvasya guptaye || 23 ||
bhūdharāya bhujaṅgasya mahākopacchide'cirāt ||
bhūtanāthāya bhūtānāmādhārāya namo namaḥ || 24 ||
vaikuṇṭhāya viśiṣṭānāṃ viśiṣṭajñānadāyine ||

kṣīrodaśāyine sākṣātkṣīrodasyāpi hetave ||
nirādhārāya nityāya nityānandāya te namaḥ || 26 ||
yajñarūpāya yajñasya phalaprāptyekahetave ||
yajñānāṃ pataye tubhyaṃ yajñagamyāya te namaḥ || 27 ||
janārdanāya daityānāṃ śatrave śaktidāyine ||
svabhaktānāṃ viśuddhānāṃ viśeṣeṇa namo namaḥ || 28 ||
vāsudevāya vasvādidāyine vāsavādibhiḥ ||
pūjitāya purāṇāya puṃse pūrṇātmane namaḥ || 29 ||
dāmodarāya devānāṃ śatrunāśaikahetave ||
dāntacittajanasyāsya rakṣakāya namo namaḥ || 30 ||
acyutāyākhilasyāsya sākṣiṇe'cyutavastubhiḥ ||
asaktāya susakāya svasaṃvedyāya te namaḥ || 31 ||
haraye hārakeyūrakaṭakādivibhūṣaṇaiḥ ||
alaṃkṛtāya kalyāṇaśarīrāya namo namaḥ || 32 ||

nānāvidhasya jagataḥ sthitikāraṇāya ||

evaṃ bhaktyā hariṃ stutvā satyasaṃdho mahādvijaḥ ||

satyasaṃdha mahābhakta mama satyaparāyaṇa ||

brahmādidevatāśvānyā naiva saṃsāramocakāḥ || 39 ||
śiva eva hi jantūnāṃ mahāsaṃsāravartinām ||

mahādevaṃ samāśritya vāñchitaṃ nā''pnuyādyadi ||

sarvamuktaṃ samāsena mama bhaktasya te'nagha ||

\ bhaktirbahuvidhā jñeyā bhavānīsahitasya tu ||
ekā śaṃkarasāyujyaśravā sāratarā parā || 2 ||
anyā śaṃkarasārūpya śradvā'tīva śivapriyā ||
aparā śivasāmīpyaśraddhā vedavidāṃ varāḥ ||
itarā śivasālokyaśraddhā'bhīṣṭaphalapradā || 3 ||
aparā ca śivajñāna śraddhā pāśanikṛntanī || 4 ||
janyā vedaśiraḥśraddhā sākṣāddijñānadāyinī ||
aparā śravaṇaśraddhā proktā vedāntavedibhiḥ || 5 ||
itarā mananaśraddhā nṛṇāṃ saṃbhāvanāpradā ||
anyā deveśvaradhyāna śraddhārūpā mahattarā || 6 ||
aparodūlanaśraddhā bhasmanā pāpanāśinī ||
tripuṇḍadhāraṇā tadanyā tattvadāyinī || 7 ||
rudrākṣadhāraṇaśraddhā cāpi bhaktirudīritā |
paḍakṣarajapaśraddhā cāpi bhaktirmahattarā || 8 ||
śivaliṅgārcana śradvā cāpimatiranuttamā |
liṅgārcanādidṛkṣā ca mahābhaktiḥ prakīrtitā || 9 ||
anumodanamīśasya pūjāyāṃ bhaktirucyate ||
pūjopakaraṇaśraddhā cāpi bhaktirudīryate || 10 ||
śivotsavadidṛkṣā ca śivabhaktirmahattarā ||
tathaivotsavasevā ca bhaktiruktā'tiśobhanā || 11 ||
tathaivotsava sevārthamāgatānāṃ mahātmanām ||
annapānapradānaṃ ca śivabhaktirudīritā || 12 ||
mahādevakathādīnāṃ śravaṇecchā maharṣayaḥ ||
mahābhaktiriti proktā mahāmāheśvarairjanaiḥ || 13 ||
kathāśravaṇakāle tu śivasya paramātmanaḥ ||
vikāraḥ svaranetrāderbhaktiruktā mahātmabhiḥ || 14 ||
udyānakaraṇaṃ śaṃbho: śivabhaktirudāhṛtā ||

pūrvoktenaiva mārgeṇa kuryādajñānanāśanam ||
jācāryācchrutavedāntaḥ satyavāggurubhaktimān || 7 ||
yo vidyāsaṃtatijñānavihīno deśiko bhavet ||
sa ghoraṃ yāti narakaṃ nāsti saṃdehakāraṇam || 8 ||
yo vidyāsaṃtatijñānavihīno deśiko bhavet ||
sa nabhobhakṣaṇenaiva vyādhiṃ vinivartayeva || 9 ||
yo vidyāsaṃtatijñānavihīno deśiko bhavet ||
sa vinaiva tilāṃstailaṃ labhate sikatāsu ca || 10 ||
yo vidyāsaṃtatijñānasahito deśiko bhavet ||
so'nāyāsena saṃsārānnṛṇāmuttārako bhavet || 11 ||
svagotrarṣiṃ namaskṛtya gurūktenaiva vartmanā ||
svaguruṃ ca namaskṛtya śradvayā ca gurorgurum || 12 ||
vighneśaṃ ṣaṇmukhaṃ cāpi śivāṃ vidyāsvarūpiṇīm ||
anyāṃśca sakalāndevānbrahmaviṣṇupurogamān || 13 ||
punaḥ śiṣyasya medhāvī cittapākaṃ parīkṣya ca ||
avidyāpāśavicchedaṃ kuryātprājñastu deśikaḥ || 14 ||
viditvā śiṣyacittasya vipākaṃ punarāstikāḥ ||
dadyātpākānurūpeṇa vidyāmetāṃ maheśvarīm || 15 ||
mūrkhaśiṣyopadeśena vidyāgarveṇa suvratāḥ ||
gurudroheṇa sarvajño'pyandhakūpe patatyadhaḥ ||16||
tasmātsaṃvatsaraṃ śiṣyaṃ parīkṣyākṛtrimaṃ punaḥ ||
pradadyādvaidikīṃ vidyāṃ gururvidyābhivṛddhaye || 17 ||
vidyāsaṃtativijñānaṃ śiṣyacittaparīkṣaṇam ||
avaśyaṃbhāvi viprendrā deśikasyeśvarājñayā || 18 ||
saṃpradāyavihīnā yā vidyā vedāntapāragāḥ ||
sā'vidyā naiva vidyā syāditi tattvavidāṃ sthitiḥ||19||
pāraṃparyaparijñānaṃ paravidyāpravartakam ||
pāraṃparyāvabodhena vidyā sā vīryavattarā || 20 ||
pāraṃparyaparijñānādeva pāśanikṛntanam ||
tasmātprājñaḥ svavidyāyāḥ saṃtatijñānavānbhavet ||21||
yathā gotraparijñānaṃ vivāhasyopakārakam ||
pāraṃparyaparijñānaṃ tathā jñānopakārakam || 22 ||
vidyāsaṃtatayo viprā bahurūpāḥ śrutau śrutāḥ ||
tattatsaṃtativijñānaṃ vidyāsiddhestu kāraṇam || 23 ||
tasya bhaktisahitasya bodhayet || 24 ||
śuddhavaṃśaparavedanena tu || 25 ||
svakaṃ vapustasya dadāti citsukham || 26 ||
na deśikatvaṃ na sukhitvamāstikāḥ ||27||

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi sadyomuktikaraṃ param ||
āmnāyāntaikasaṃsiddhaṃ sukaraṃ sarvadehinām || 1 ||
purā bhagavatī devī bhogamokṣaphalapradā ||
purāṇī pūrṇavijñānasvarūpā paramā śivā || 2 ||
devadevaṃ jagannāthaṃ deveṣu ca nareṣu ca ||
krimikīṭapataṃgeṣu samaṃ sarveṣu saṃsthitam || 3 ||
satyavijñāna saṃpūrṇa sukhalakṣaṇamavyayam ||
svaprakāśaikasaṃsiddhaṃ svavilakṣaṇavarjitam || 4 ||
ghṛtakāṭhinyavaddiprāḥ kevalaṃ kṛpayaiva tu ||
āvirbhūtamahānandatāṇḍavaṃ karuṇālayam || 5 ||

devadeva jagannātha jagatāmārtibhañjana ||

hitāya jagatāṃ tasyai vabhāṣe tanmaheśvaraḥ || 8 ||

itaḥ pūrva mayā nokaṃ vadāmi tava tacchṛṇu || 9 ||
brāhmaṇo vā'ntyajo vā'pi strī pākhaṇḍo'thavā budhaḥ||
daridro vā saṃmṛddho vā mūrkho vā paṇḍito'tha vā || 10 ||

prātaḥ snātvā yathāśakti dhanaṃ dattvā priyeṇa tu ||
śrīkālahasthināthākhyaṃ devi māmādareṇa tu || 17 ||
pradakṣiṇaṃ yathāśakti kṛtvā bhūmau tu daṇḍavat ||
praṇamya dṛṣṭvā deveśi naktabhojanamācaret || 18 ||
āditye vṛṣabhaṃ prāpte viśākha samāhitaḥ |
suvarṇamukharītoye prātaḥ snātvā yathābalam || 19 ||
dattvā pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā devaṃ dṛṣṭvā'bhivandya ca ||
'samāhitamanā bhūtvā natabhojanamācaret || 20 ||
māditye mithunaṃ prāpte mūlākhye tārake budhaḥ ||
suvarṇamukharīsnānaṃ kṛtvā prātaḥ samāhitaḥ || 21 ||
pradattvā dhanamanyaddā yathāśakti maharṣayaḥ ||
devaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya praṇamya bhuvi daṇḍavat ||
dṛṣṭā tathaiva māṃ devi nakabhojanamācaret || 22 ||
āditye karkaṭaṃ prāpte garbha susamāhitaḥ || 23 ||
suvarṇamukharīsnānaṃ kṛtvā prātardvijottamāḥ ||
dṛṣṭvā tatraiva māṃ devi devaṃ bhaktipuraḥsaram || 24 ||
pradakṣiṇaṃ yathāśakti kṛtvā dṛṣṭvā'bhivandya ca ||
tyaktvā'harbhojanaṃ dhīmānrātrau bhojanamācareva || 25 ||
siṃharāśau sthite sūrye vaiṣṇave tārake naraḥ ||
prātareva mahānadyāmasyāṃ snātvā yathābalam || 26 ||
dattvā pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā stutvā māmabhivandya ca ||
tyaktvā'rbhojanaṃ martyo rātrau bhojanamācareva || 27 ||
vaiṣṇavaṃ śravaṇa nakṣatram | 'viṣṇurdevatā" iti śrutervaiṣṇavaṃ śravaṇākhyam ||
āditye kanyakāyukte tathā'jaikapade dine ||
srātvā cāsyāṃ naraḥ prātardattvā viprāya ojanam || 28 ||
śrīkālahastināthākhyaṃ devaṃ pūrvoktavartmanā ||
dṛṣṭvā'harbhojanaṃ tyaktvā rātrau bhojanamācaret || 29 ||
tulāṃ prāpte tu mārtaṇḍe cāśvinyāṃ prātareva ca ||
nadyāmasyāṃ naraḥ khātvā dattvā viprāya bhojanam ||30||
pradakṣiṇapraṇāmādi kṛtvā naktaṃ samācaret ||
sūrye vṛśvikasaṃyukte kṛttikāyāṃ dvijarṣabhāḥ || 31 ||

tyaktvā'harbhojanaṃ martyo rātrau bhojanamācareva || 32 ||

kṛtvā tu pūrvavadevi naktabhojanamācaret || 33 ||
sūrye makarasaṃyukte puṣyanakṣatra ke naraḥ ||
pūrvavatsakalaṃ kṛtvā naktabhojanamācaret || 34 ||

pūrvavatsakalaṃ kṛtvā rātrau bhojanamācaret || 37 ||

muktyupāyamayatnena mayā notamitaḥ purā || 1 ||
purā jaiminiratyanta śradvayā saha suvratāḥ ||
svaguruṃ vedavedāntaviśāradamanuttamam || 2 ||
tapasā dīptasarvāṅgaṃ parāśarasutaṃ prabhum ||

nidhāya mūrdhni tatpādapaṅkajaṃ bhavabheṣajam ||
apṛcchalokarakṣārthamatigṛhyamanuttamam || 4 ||
bhagavansarvajantūnāmayatnena vimuktidam ||
vada kāruṇyato nātha mama māyāviṣāpaham || 5 ||
sādhu sādhu muniśreṣṭha tvayā pṛṣṭaṃ jagadvitam ||
purā purāṇaṃ brahmāṇamidaṃ pṛṣṭaṃ mayā'pi ca || 6 ||

svasvarūpamahānandapramodajalavisthitaḥ ||

tatra māmādareṇaiva nṛtyamānaṃ dine dine ||

śṛṇutātipriyeṇaiva dvijāḥ sāratarottamam || 1 ||
purā satyavatīsūnuḥ sarvavijñānasāgaraḥ ||
sarvavedodadheḥ pāro gururme karuṇānidhiḥ || 2 ||
sarvalokopakārāya sāmvaṃ saṃsārabheṣajam ||
dhyāyamāno mahābhaktyā tatāpa paramaṃ tapaḥ || 3 ||
punaḥ puṣpādibhirdevaṃ samārādhya yathābalam ||
paḍakṣareṇa mantreṇa tuṣṭāvaṃ ca maheśvaram || 4 ||
paratattvāya tattvānāṃ tattvabhūtāya vastutaḥ ||
svasmādanyavihīnāya namastasmai svayaṃbhuve || 5 ||

virāḍādyāśva devāśca yanmātraṃ taṃ numaḥ śivam || 7 ||

yatsvarūpamavijñāya dehamātmeti manvate ||
tarkābhāsaistamīśānaṃ vande dehavilakṣaṇam || 18 ||
. yatsvarūpamavijñāya dehajānīndriyāṇi tu ||

yatsvarūpamavijñāya manaḥ saṃkalpalakṣaṇam ||

antaḥkaraṇamātmeti manvate taṃ numaḥ śivam || 23 ||

yasminsvapraprapañco'yaṃ bhātīva bhavatīva ca || .
taṃ tadbhrānteradhiṣṭhānaṃ vande sākṣiṇamīśvaram || 25 ||
yasminsuṣuptyavastheyaṃ bhātīva bhavatīva ca ||
taṃ tadbhrānteradhiṣṭhānaṃ vande sākṣiṇamīśvaram || 26 ||
yasmintaṃ turīyatvaṃ tridhāmāpekṣayaiva tu ||
taṃ turīyatvanirmuktaṃ vande cidanamīśvaram || 27 ||
yasmiṃsturīyātītatvamadhyastaṃ tadbhāvataḥ || -
taṃ vande kevalaṃ śuddhaṃ nirviśeṣaṃ maheśvaram || 28 ||

abhinaṃ ca tathā bhinaṃ bhinnābhinnaṃ vadanti yam ||
taṃ sadā kevalaṃ vande keṣāṃ cillabhyamīśvaram || 30 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ namaḥ paramāiyam || 31 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ sadeśvarasadāśivo ||
yathārthe brahma jānītastaṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 32 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ sarvadevānaśaṅkitāḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 33 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vibhinnāñjīvacetanān ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramāddayam || 34 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ sarvavedānaśaṅkitāḥ ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramāddayam || 35 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ smṛtīḥ sarvā aśaṅkitāḥ ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 36 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ purāṇāni ca bhāratam ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 37 ||

yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vividhānvaiṣṇavāgamān ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādvayam || 39 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā brāhmānetāṃstathā''gamān ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādvayam || 40 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā buddhārhatāgamānimān ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramāddayam || 41 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ śabdānsatyetarādikān ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 42 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vidyāḥ sarvā aśaṅkitāḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramāddayam || 43 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāstarkāninyonyavādhakān ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādvayam || 44 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā mānamadhyakṣapūrvakam ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādyayam || 45 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā brāhmaṇānkṣatriyānviśaḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādvayam || 46 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ śūdrānapi ca saṃkarān ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 47 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā āśramānakhilānapi ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 48 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā dharmādharmānaśaṅkitāḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 49 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā varjyāvarjyānaśaṅkitāḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramāhvayam || 50 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vidyāvidyā aśaṅkitāḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ namaḥ paramāddayam || 51 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā dehādīnakhilānimān ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ namaḥ paramādayam || 52 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā jāgradāditrayaṃ sadā ||
yathārthe brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādvayam || 53 ||
yathārthe brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādvayam || 54 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā bhūmiṃ tadamāstikāḥ ||
yathārthe brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramāiyam || 55 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā jalaṃ tadvedamāstikāḥ ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramāiyam || 56 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā agniṃ tadvedamāstikāḥ ||
yathārthe brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramāddayam || 57 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā vāyuṃ tadvedamāstikāḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādvayam || 58 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā ākāśaṃ tatra kalpitam ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 59 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ śabdasparśādikānimān ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 60 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā mahadādyakhilaṃ jagat ||
yathārtha brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 61 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ sarvametadaśaṅkitāḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādvayam || 62 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannā mahāmāyāmaśaṅkitāḥ ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 63 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāśvicchaktiṃ vimalāmimām ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ numaḥ paramādvayam || 64 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ pratītamakhilaṃ jagat ||
yathārthaṃ brahma jānanti taṃ namaḥ paramādayam || 65 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ phalāvāpyai kadācana ||
na kiṃcidapi kurvanti taṃ numaḥ paramādayam || 66 ||
yasya vijñānasaṃpannāḥ pratyagjyotiṣi saṃsthitāḥ ||
tameva pratyagātmānaṃ vande'haṃtādivarjitam || 67 ||
idaṃrūpamahaṃrūpaṃ yasya bhāti tamīśvaram ||
vande lakṣaṇamadvaṃdvamanirdeśyaṃ svayaṃprabham || 68 ||
nikhilajagadrahitaṃ namāmi śaśvat || 69 ||
evaṃ vyāsena sarvajñaḥ sāmbaḥ sarvaphalapradaḥ ||
abhiṣṭuto mahādevaḥ pratyakṣamabhavanmune || 70 ||
taṃ dṛṣṭvā devadeveśaṃ devyā sahitamavyayam ||
praṇamya prārthayāmāsa sarvasādhanavedanam || 71 ||
devadevo'pi sarvajñaḥ prasannaḥ sarvasādhanam ||
prāha gambhīrayā vācā munaye munisattamāḥ || 72 ||
vakṣye vima samāsena sarvasādhanamuttamam ||
śṛṇuṣva śraddhayā sārdhaṃ mayā noktamitaḥ purā || 73 ||
apekṣitārthaḥ sarveṣāṃ bhuktirmuktiśca suvratāḥ ||
muktirnānāvidhā proktā mayā vedānusārataḥ || 74 ||
taṃtra sāyujyarūpāyā mukteḥ sākṣāttu sādhanam ||
samyagjñānaṃ na karmoktaṃ na tayośva samuccayaḥ || 75 ||
nityasiddhā'thavā muktiḥ sādhyarūpā'dvayī gatiḥ ||
nityasiddhā tu sarveṣāmātmarūpā'thavā'parā || 76 ||
ātmarūpaiva cenmuktirnityaprāptā hi sā''tmanaḥ ||
nityaprāptasya cāprāptirvibhramaḥ khalu dehinām || 77 ||
viśvamasya nivṛttyā sā prāpteti vyapadiśyate ||
vibhramasya nivṛttistu sidhyatyajñānanāśataḥ || 78 ||
ajñānasya vināśastu jñānādeva na cānyataḥ ||
jñānādajñānanāśastu prasiddhaḥ sarvadehinām || 79 ||
prasiddheti darśayati - jñānādivi || 72 ||
prāpyā cedātmanā muktiraprāptaprāptireva sā ||
aprāptaprāptirapyasya saṃbandho vaikyameva vā || 81 ||
anityaḥ sa tu saṃbandho bhavennityo na sarvathā || 82 ||
sādhyānāmapi bhāvānāmanityatvaṃ vyavasthitam ||
abhāvasya na sādhyatvaṃ pradhvaṃsākhyasya sarvadā || 83 ||
sādhyatvākhyastu dharmaśca naivābhāvāśrayo bhavet ||
nityo yadi sa saṃbandhastarhi saṃbandhasaṃjñitā || 84 ||
muktiśca nityasidvaiva mumukṣorātmano bhavet ||
tadā'pi nityaprāptāyā muktaḥ prāptistu pūrvavat ||
vijñānenaiva nānyena satyamuktaṃ dvijottama || 85 ||
aprāptaprāptirūpāyā mukteraikyaṃ bhavedyadi || 86 ||
tana yuktaṃ dvayoraikyaṃ na sidhyati kadācana ||
bhinnayorbhedanāśe vā muktirbhede sthite'thavā || 87 ||
bhedanāśe tayoraikyaṃ ghaṭate vedavittama ||
bhede sati tayoraikyamiti cetanna saṃgatam || 88 ||
bhedasya saṃnidhāvaikyaṃ virodhānnaiva sidhyati ||
na prāpyā hyātmanā muktiriti cettanna saṃgatam || 89 ||
aprāpyāyāstu mukteśva nāstyapekṣā hi sādhane ||
sādhane sati sā muktiramāpyaiva sadā khalu || 90 ||
na nityasiddhā sā muktiḥ sādhyarūpaiva cenmatam ||
sādhyatve satyanityatvaṃ pūrvamevābhibhāṣitam || 91 ||
pradhvaṃsasya tu nityatvaṃ sarvathā na bhaviṣyatei ||
acidrapasya sarvasya vināśo gamyate yataḥ || 92 ||
bhāvatve sati sādhyatvādvināśo'cetanasya tu ||
pradhvaṃsasya tu sādhyatve'pyabhāvatvena hetunā || 93 ||
na sidhyati vināśastu tacca naiva susaṃgatam ||
prāgabhāvasamākhyasyāpyanityatvasya darśanāt || 94 ||
prāgabhāvasya sādhyatvābhāve satyapyabhāvataḥ ||
anityatvaṃ yadīṣyeta pradhvaṃsasyāpi tatsamam || 95 ||
bhāvānāmapyabhāvānāṃ sādhyānāṃ munisattama ||
asādhyānāṃ ca sarveṣāmanityatve prayojakam || 96 ||
acetanatvamevoktaṃ netaravyabhicārataḥ ||
cetanasya tu nityatvaṃ śrutirāha sanātanī || 97 ||
tasmāduktaprakāreṇa muktiḥ sāyujyarūpiṇī ||
jñānalabhyā kriyāmātrānna labhyā na samuccayāt ||98||
jñānaṃ nāmākhilaṃ cedaṃ sadrūpeṇāvabhāsanam ||
kriyā tu kārakāpekṣā na jñānālambinī sadā ||99||
jataḥ kriyāyā jñānena virodhādeva sarvadā ||
samuccayo na yujyeta kutastena parā gatiḥ || 100 ||
sārūpyākhyā tu yā muktiḥ sāmīpyākhyā ca yā'parā ||
sālokyākhyā ca yā tāsāṃ kevalaṃ karma sādhanam || 101 ||
aihikāmuṣmikākārā muktayaḥ sarvadehinām ||
karmaṇaiva hi sidhyanti na jñānena virodhataḥ || 102 ||
jñānaṃ karma ca vedoktameva nānyoditaṃ bhavet ||
anyoditaṃ tu viprendra vyavahāre'vivekinām || 103 ||
apekṣya buddhi vijñānaṃ karma ceti vidhīyate ||
tathā'pi vyavahāre te vyāvahārikasiddhide || 104 ||
tasmātsarvatra nāstikyaṃ na kuryānmatimattamaḥ ||
nāstikyādeva sarveṣāṃ saṃsāre parivartanam || 105 ||
sarvamuktaṃ samāsena sādhanaṃ munisattama ||
gopanīyamidaṃ tasmādāstikasya sadā'dbhutam ||106 ||
evamuktvā mahādevaḥ sāmbaḥ sarvāvabhāsakaḥ ||
pranṛtya saṃnidhau tasya tatraivāntarhito'bhavat || 107 ||
moha eva hi samastamito'nyathā || 108 ||
muktisādhanavicāro nāmāṣṭātriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 38 ||
sādhanavicāro nāmāṣṭātriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 38 ||
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi samāsena na vistarāt ||
avirodhaṃ tu vedānāmaśeṣāṇāṃ munīśvarāḥ || 1 ||
dvividho vedarāśistu munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ||
satyādvaitaparaḥ kaśvidvedabhāgaḥ samāsataḥ || 2 ||
kalpitadetaniṣṭhastu vedabhāgo'parastathā ||
satyameva sadā'dvaitamasatyaṃ dvaitamāstikāḥ || 3 ||
dvaitasyāpi ca satyatvaṃ varṇayantīha kecana ||
tadusaṃgatamadhyastaṃ dvaitaṃ yasmātparātmani || 4 ||
abhyastaṃ hi sadā dvaitaṃ dṛśyatvācchuktirūpyavat ||
dṛśyatvaṃ dvaitajātasya saṃmataṃ sarvadehinām || 5||
tasmādvaitaparo bhāgaḥ kalpitadvaitagocaraḥ ||
advaitaṃ sarvadā satyaṃ bhedābhāvātkathaṃcana || 6 ||
advaitamapi cādhyastaṃ yadi vedavidāṃ varāḥ ||
kutraivādvaitamadhyastaṃ nādvaite tadabhāvataḥ || 7 ||
kevala kalpite te nādvaitābhyāsa saṃbhavaḥ ||
vyavahāradaśāyāṃ tu satye'dhyāsasya darśanāt || 8 ||
dvaite cādvaitamadhyastamiti vaktuṃ na śakyate ||
tasyābhyāsasvarūpatvādvaitasya brahmavittamāḥ || 9 ||
dvaitaṃ cāpi tathā'dvaitamubhayaṃ kalpitaṃ na hi ||
dvaitādvaitātirekeṇa nāstitvādeva vastunaḥ || 10 ||
śūnyamātre na cādhyastamubhayaṃ vedavittamāḥ ||
nirupākhyasya cādhyāsāviṣṭhānatvādyasaṃbhavāt || 11 ||
ato dvaitaṃ samabhyastamadvitīye parātmani ||
tasmāduktena mārgeṇa kaśvidaṃśaḥ śruterbudhāḥ || 12 ||
satyādvaitaparaḥ proktaḥ sarvaśāstrārthavedibhiḥ ||
tathaiva vedurāśestu kaśvidaṃśastapodhanāḥ ||
kalpitadetaniṣṭhastu kathitaḥ satyavādibhiḥ || 13 ||
dvaitādvaitaśrutīnāṃ tu virodho'pi pratītitaḥ ||
uktenaiva prakāreṇa virodhābhāva eva hi || 14 ||
pratyakṣāderagamyatvādadvaitasya tu sarvadā ||
tatraivārthavatī sākṣādadvaitaśrutirāstikāḥ || 15 ||
antareṇa śrutiṃ bhedo lokasiddhaḥ sadaiva tu || 16 ||
tena nārthavatī tatra śrutirmānātigāminī ||
pramāṇāntarasaṃvādāpekṣā nāsti śruteḥ sadā || 17 ||
svataśca parato doṣo nāsti tasyāḥ śruterapi ||
pratyakṣādipramāṇānāṃ doṣavadbhāvatā sadā ||
astyataḥ śrutireteṣāṃ pramāṇānāṃ balīyasī || 18 ||
kalpitatamātre tu naiva mānamiyaṃ śrutiḥ ||
tatra prayojanābhāvātparamārthanirūpaṇe || 19 ||
advaitaṃ paramānandaṃ brahmavastu na cāparam ||
tatra prayojanaṃ viprā astyeva hi na saṃśayaḥ || 20 ||
yatra prayojanaṃ tatra śrutirmānamiti sthitiḥ || 21 ||
ataḥ prayojanābhāvādvaitaṃ na pratipādyate ||
anūdya dvaitamadvaitaṃ pratipādayati śrutiḥ || 22 ||
smṛtīnāṃ ca purāṇānāṃ bhāratādestathaiva ca ||
tathā śaivāgamādīnāṃ tarkāṇāṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ||
advaitaniṣṭhataivoktā na dvaitaparatā sadā || 23 ||
abhyastājñānatatkāryanivṛttidvārato'dvayam ||
vodhayanti mudā kāśvicchūtayaḥ paṇḍiteottamāḥ || 24 ||
sākṣāddidhimukhenaiva brahma satyādilakṣaṇam ||
bodhayanti mudā kāścicchūtayaḥ paṇḍitottamāḥ ||25||
sādhakasyaiva jīvasya svābhāvikaśivātmatām ||
vodhayantī śrutirbhrāntajīvatvaṃ bādhate khalu || 26 ||
jīvatvaṃ cetanasyāsya svābhāvikamiti dvijāḥ ||
keciddadanti vārtepā na tatsvābhāvikaṃ sadā || 27 ||
yadi svābhāvikaṃ tarhi jīvatvaṃ sarvadā bhavet ||
nāsti tasya nivṛttirhi svataḥ siddhaṃ na naśyati || 28 ||
yathā bheṣajasaṃparkāttāmrasya malanāśanam ||
tathā jīvasya duḥkhādinivṛttiḥ kenacidbhavet || 29 ||
rasaviddhamayaḥ svarṇe yathā bhavati sarvadā ||
kenacitsādhanenaiva tathā jīvaḥ śivo bhavet ||
iti kecitsvamohena pravadanti tu vādinaḥ || 30 ||
tanna saṃpratipannaṃ hi svataḥ siddhaṃ na naśyati || 31 ||
yathā svābhāvika herauṣṇyaṃ naiva vinaśyati ||
prakāśo vā tathā'syāpi na duḥkhādirvinaśyati || 32 ||
maṇimantraupadhādīnāṃ śaktivaicitryamātrataḥ ||
neṣṭavatprativaddhaṃ tu na naṣṭaṃ saṃmataṃ hi tat || 33 ||
yathā tāmramalaṃ naiva kenacitpravinaśyati ||
naṣṭayatprativaddhaṃ hi vinaṣṭaṃ manyate'budhāḥ || 34 ||
jīvatvaṃ ca tathā'syāpi sukhaduḥkhādilakṣaṇam ||
naṣṭavatpratibaddhaṃ syānnaiva naśyati kenacit || 35 ||
payasā veṣṭitaṃ toyaṃ paya ityabhidhīyate || 36 ||
rajataṃ kāñcanagrastaṃ hema ityabhidhīyate ||
tathaiva rasavīryeṇa vahnisaṃparkato'pi ca || 37 ||
jayaso hemavarṇatvaṃ na hematvaṃ kadācana ||
rasavīryavināśe tu varṇastasya vinaśyati || 38 ||
kṛtakasya na nityatvamiti vārtā bhuvi sthirā ||
tathā'pi mānavā śrāntāḥ kāñcanaṃ manyate hyayaḥ || 39||
sūkṣmadarśanahīnānāṃ sulabhaḥ khalu vibhramaḥ ||
tathā śivatvaṃ jīvasya śrānyā siddhaṃ bhaviṣyati || 40 ||
sādhanena svato jīvo na śivaḥ sarvathā bhavet ||
tato jīvaḥ śivaḥ sākṣātra bhavettu kadācana ||
śiva eva svataḥ sākṣācchivo bhavati nānyathā ||41||
yathaiva vahnisaṃparkāttoyaṃ vahnirna vastutaḥ ||
uṣṇaṃ toyamiti prājñāḥ pratītāvapi dehinām || 42 ||
tathā'śivaḥ svato jīvaḥ kadācitpaṇḍitottamāḥ ||
śivatvena pratīto'pi svato naiva śivo bhavet || 43 ||
svato'śivastu jīvo'yaṃ savarthā na śivo bhavet || 44 ||
kenacitsādhanenaiva muktau śivasamo bhavet ||
ityevaṃ kecidicchanti vādino munipuṅgavāḥ || 45 ||
vārtāmātramidaṃ proktaṃ sarvathā na tadarthavat ||
ekadeśena vā jīvāḥ kiṃvā sarvātmanā samaḥ || 46 ||
ekadeśena cetsarve śivāḥ saṃsāravartinaḥ ||
ekadeśena sarvepāmasti sāmyaṃ śivena hi || 47 ||
sarvātmanā cetsāmyaṃ tatsarvathā śiva eva saḥ ||
bhedakāraṇaśūnyatvādbhedābhāvācca vastutaḥ || 48 ||
kiṃca muktau śivenaiva samo jīvo bhavedyadi ||
kaṃcitkālaṃ hi tatsāmyamāgataṃ khalu gacchati ||49||
tasmājjīvaḥ svataḥ sākṣācchivaḥ satyādilakṣaṇaḥ ||
apracyutātmabhāvena sthitaḥ sanparavidyayā || 50 ||
svājñānaṃ tatprasūtaṃ ca saṃsāraṃ svātmanā grasan ||
svapūrṇaśivarūpeṇa svayamevāvaśiṣyate || 51 ||
śuktikākaladhautaṃ tu śuktikāvedanena tu ||
śuktikāmātrarūpeṇa yathā loke'vaśiṣyate || 52 ||
śivātmanā jagadbādho na caivaṃ saṃbhaviṣyati ||
abhāva eva muktau tu jagato hi bhaviṣyati || 53 ||
ityevaṃ kecidicchanti sa ca mandamatibhramaḥ ||
bhāvarūpaṃ tu vastveva bhāvi bhavati dvijāḥ || 54 ||
jaganna bhāvo nābhāvo bhāvābhāvavilakṣaṇam ||
tasmāddhyastabādhastu na bhāvo'bhāva eva na || 55 ||
adhiṣṭhānāvaśeṣo hi kevalaṃ paṇḍitottamāḥ ||
jagadbhramasyādhiṣṭhānaṃ śivaḥ satyasvabhāvataḥ || 56 ||
tadanyadakhilaṃ bhrāntaṃ yuktitaśca pramāṇataḥ ||
tasmātsarvajagadvādhe śiva evāvaśiṣyate || 57 ||
śivāvaśeṣaṃ sarvasya jagataḥ śrutirādarāt ||
vakti tatra na saṃdehastrirvaḥ śapathayāmyaham || 58 ||
tasmātsatyaparānandaprakāśādvaitamīśvaram ||
vodhayantyādareṇaiva śrutayaḥ smṛtibhiḥ saha || 59 ||
ekatvavodhakasyāsya vedavākyasya suvratāḥ ||
vākyāntarāṇi sarvāṇi śepabhūtāni saṃtatam || 60 ||
vedo nānyasya śepastu yathā devo maheśvaraḥ ||
śivasya śepaṃ sakalaṃ śrutermānāni sarvaśaḥ || 61 ||
yathā mātā svaputrasya satyamevābhibhāṣate ||
tathā sarvajanasyāpi satyaṃ vadati hi śrutiḥ || 62 ||
śrutau cāpi mahādeve tripuṇḍre bhasmaguṇṭhane ||
śraddhāṃ na kurute martyaḥ puṇyaleśavivarjitaḥ || 63 ||
pāpiṣṭhānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tripuṇḍrolane śrutau ||
mahādeve ca vidveṣaḥ svata eva vijāyate || 64 ||
vedotkarṣe śivotkarṣe vidyotkarṣe tathaiva ca ||
tripuṇḍroḍūlanotkarṣe śraddhā puṇyavatāṃ bhavet || 65 ||
avirodhe tu vedānāṃ puroktenaiva vartmanā ||
vedānusārismṛtyādau pāpiṣṭasya na hi spṛhā || 66||
viṣṇvādeḥ śivasāmyatve vedasāmye parasya ca ||
kurvantīcchā mavidvāṃsaḥ pāpamevātra kāraṇam || 67 ||
vedānāmapakarpe tu tripuṇḍrādestathaiva ca ||
tathā śivāpakarṣe ca yatante pāpayonayaḥ || 68 ||
mahādevaśva vedaśva tathā tiryaktrapuṇḍrakam ||
vyarthamityāhuratyartha pāpaṇḍāḥ pāpayonayaḥ || 69 ||
mahādevasya māhātmyaṃ vedānāmapi vaibhavam ||
tripuṇḍrasya ca māhātmyaṃ na śakyaṃ varṇituṃ mayā || 70 ||
karmaśeṣatvamāyāsādbrahmakāṇḍasya kecana ||
varṇayanti na te santaḥ kiṃtu te vipralambhakāḥ || 71 ||
kartṛtvaṃ caiva bhoktṛtvaṃ niyojyatvaṃ kriyāphalam ||
grasate brahmavijñānaṃ tatastaccheṣatā'sya na || 72 ||
alpalābhapradaṃ karma jñānaṃ pūrṇaphalapradam ||
tathā sati muniśreṣṭhāstacchepatvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet || 73 ||
phalavatkarmaśepatvamaphalasya hi sidhyati ||
phalavāda paraṃ jñānaṃ tatastaccheṣatā'sya na || 74 ||
karmaprakaraṇasthaṃ hi jñānaṃ karmāṅgamiṣyate ||
