rajjuvālaṃ ca dātyūhaṃ śukaṃ sārikasaṃjñitam ||
pratudājñjālapādāṃśca brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet || 37 ||
turaṅgasya gajasyāpi maṇḍukasya tathaiva ca ||
purīpaṃ ca tathā mūtraṃ brāhmaṇo naiva akṣayet || 38 ||
narāṇāṃ ca gajānāṃ ca māṃsamaśvasya sattamāḥ ||
mahiṣasya ca māṃsaṃ ca brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet || 39 ||
ajāvimāṃsaṃ raktaṃ ca gomāṃsaṃ ca tathaiva ca ||
mṛgāṇāṃ ca tathā māṃsaṃ brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayeva || 40 ||
māṃsaṃ pañcanakhānāṃ ca vinaiva sakalāni tu ||
kāmato'kāmato vā'pi brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet || 41 ||
matsyaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dṛtispṛṣṭamājyaṃ kīlālameva ca ||
rasaṃ tālaphalasyāpi brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet || 42 ||
odanaṃ tu punaḥpakkaṃ nālikerarasaṃ tathā ||
pakkaṃ toyamabhūmisthaṃ brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayeva || 43 ||
anirdaśāhagokṣīramauṭramekaśaphaṃ tathā ||
āvikaṃ saṃdhinīkṣīraṃ vivatsāyāśca goḥ payaḥ || 44 ||
āraṇyānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ mṛgāṇāṃ mahiṣīṃ vinā ||
strīkṣīraṃ ca śramādā'pi brāhmaṇo na pivetsadā || 45 ||
gogajāśvādibhirghātaṃ pādaspṛṣṭaṃ ca kāmataḥ ||
anulomādibhiḥ spṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇo naiva bhakṣayet || 46 ||
uktānyetāni sarvāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||
abhakṣyāṇi mayoktāni bhakṣakāśca patantyadhaḥ || 47 ||
tasmādabhakṣyaṃ saṃtyajya brāhmaṇo matimattamaḥ ||
cittasya pariśuddhyarthe bhakṣyameva tu bhakṣayet || 48 ||
kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca vaiśyānāṃ bhakṣyameṣvapi vidyate ||
tathā'pi bhakṣaṇābhāvasteṣāmatyantaśobhanaḥ || 49 ||
śūdrādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāmabhakṣyaṃ naiva vidyate ||
tathā'pyabhakṣaṇaṃ teṣāṃ phalāya mahate bhavet || 50 ||
bhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇādeva viśuddhahṛdayaḥ pumān ||
pārameśvaravijñānānmucyate bhavavandhanāt || 51 ||
parameśvaravijñānaṃ vedādeva na cānyataḥ ||
āgamāntarajanyaṃ tu jñānaṃ na jñānamāstikāḥ || 52 ||
aṣṭādaśānāṃ vidyānāṃ vedādanyāśca sattamāḥ ||
vidyā vedānusāreṇa pravṛttāḥ sarvaśobhanāḥ || 53 ||
tathā'pi tāsu sarvāsu kaścidaśaḥ kvacitkvacit ||
śivāgamānusāreṇa tatprabhedānusārataḥ || 54 ||
viṣṇvāgamānusāreṇa tatprabhedānusārataḥ ||
brahmāgamānusāreṇa tatprabhedānusārataḥ || 55 ||
adhikāriviśeṣeṇa krameṇaiva vimuktaye ||
pravartante muniśreṣṭhāḥ satyameva mayoditam || 56 ||
tattattantreṣu ye martyā dīkṣitā munisattamāḥ ||
soṃ'śastaireva saṃgrāhyaḥ sarvathā naiva vaidikaiḥ || 57 ||
maduktā saṃhitā sādhvī vedamānānusāriṇī ||
vedetarāgamādhīnaḥ kaśvideśo na vidyate || 58 ||
prasādādeva rudrasya saṃhiteyaṃ mayoditā ||
prasādaḥ śāṃkaraḥ samyagjñānasya khalu sādhanam || 59 ||
ato vedānusāreṇa dvijānāmātmaśuddhaye ||
abhakṣyamādareṇoktaṃ mayā vedārthavittamāḥ || 60 ||
sarvamuktaṃ samāsena kevalaṃ karuṇābalā ||
śraddadhānastvabhakṣyāṇi śramāddā'pi na akṣayet || 61 ||
abhakṣyanivṛttikathanaṃ nāma pañcacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 45 ||
pañcacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 45 ||
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi samāsena na vistarāt ||
yena jñānaviśeṣeṇa mṛtyuṃ paśyanti dehinaḥ || 1 ||
somacchāyāṃ dhruvaṃ caiva mahāpathamarundhatīm ||
apaśyanvatsarādūrdhvaṃ na jīvati na saṃśayaḥ || 2 ||
araśmimantamādityaṃ raśmimantaṃ ca pāvakam ||
paśyannekādaśānmāsādūrdhvaṃ maryo na jīvati || 3 ||
rajataṃ vā suvarṇa vā viṇmūtraṃ vā vamennaraḥ ||
pratyakṣamathavā svane daśa māsāna jīvati || 4 ||
bhūtapretapiśācāṃśca gandharvanagarāṇi ca ||
rukmavarṇāndramānpaśyannava māsānna jīvati || 5 ||
sthūlo vā'pi kṛśo'kasmādbhavenmartyaḥ svayaṃ yadi ||
kṛṣṇavarṇo'thavā māsānaṣṭau jīvati mānavaḥ || 6 ||
svapādaṃ khaṇḍitaṃ paśyannagrataḥ pṛṣṭhato'pi vā ||
pate vā pāṃsuke vā'pi sapta māsānna jīvati || 7 ||
kapoto vā'tha gṛno vā kāko vā yadi mūrdhani ||
sthitaḥ kravyādasaṃjño vā paṇmāsena vinaśyati || 8 ||
* gacchantī vāyasī paṅktiḥ pāṃsuvarṣe vimuñcati ||
'gaccheddāyasapaṅkībhiḥ pāṃsuvarṣeṇa vā naraḥ ||
svacchāyāṃ vikṛtāṃ paśyeccaturvā pañca jīvati || 9 ||
vidyutaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge paśyanmedhavivarjite ||
udake cāpamaindraṃ vā trīṇi hauṃ vā sa jīvati || 10 ||
darpaṇe vā jale vā'pi pareṣāṃ vā'tha cakṣupi ||
aśiraskaṃ tathā''tmānaṃ paśyanmāsena naśyati ||11||
vastagandhastu vā dehaḥ śavagandhastu vā bhavet ||
nimbagandhastu vā'tīva māsārdhena vinaśyati || 12 ||
śuṣyate hṛdayaṃ yasya mastakaṃ dhūmasaṃvṛtam ||
sadā kampo bhavedyasya daśāhaṃ naiva jīvati || 13 ||
saṃbhinno māruto yasya marmasthānāni kṛntati ||
adbhiḥ spṛṣṭo na hṛpyecca mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ ||14||
ṛkṣavānarasaṃyuktarathenaiva tu dakṣiṇām ||
diśaṃ gacchati yo martyo mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ ||15||
kṛṣṇāḥ kṛṣṇāmbarāḥ khame śmāmavastradharāḥ striyaḥ ||
yenaiva saha gacchanti dakṣiṇāṃ na sa jīvati || 16 ||
chinnaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ svakaṃ vāsaḥ svame paśyati yaḥ pumān ||
nagnaṃ vā śramaṇaṃ tasya gṛhe mṛtyurupasthitaḥ || 17 ||
nakṣatrāṇi divā paśyanrātrau cendradhanustathā ||
candraṃ raktaṃ tu vā kṛṣṇaṃ bhānuṃ paśyati mānavaḥ || 18 ||
ādityamaṇḍale paśyetsuṣiraṃ candramaṇḍale |
ākāśe raktamālāṃ vā sadya eva vinaśyati || 19 ||
śmaśānaṃ bhasma keśāṃśca nadīṃ śuṣkī bhujaṃgamān ||
paśyetsvapradaśāyāṃ yastasya mṛtyurgṛhaṃ gataḥ || 20 ||
kṛṣṇairvikeśaiḥ puruṣaiḥ svapre yaḥ pīḍitaḥ pumān ||
pāpāṇaistāḍyate yastu mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ || 21 ||
ādityodayavelāyāṃ pratyakṣaṃ yasya vai śivāḥ ||
krośantyabhimukhā hyetya mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ || 22 ||
bhayakampādayo yasya bhūyo bhūyo bhavanti ca ||
śokamohau sadā yasya mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ || 23 ||
nirjalā yasya jihvā tu dantavarṣastu yasya ca ||
hṛdaye yasya vai vahnirmṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ || 24 ||
cakṣurekaṃ sravedyasya karṇau sthānācca bhraśyataḥ ||
yasya nāsā ca cakrā syānmṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ||25||
yasya jihvā ca kṛṣṇā syātsumukhaṃ durmukhaṃ bhavet ||
gaṇḍe ca kṛṣṇe rakte vā mṛtyustasya gṛhaṃ gataḥ || 26 ||
muktakeśī hasangāyannṛtyangacchati dakṣiṇām ||
diśaṃ svapre'sya mṛtyuḥ syādīdṛśasvapradarśinaḥ || 27 ||
śvetabhūtāstathā śvetā aśvāḥ śvetatarā api ||
vahanti yāmyadeśe yaṃ tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ || 28 ||
utarāsabhasaṃyuktaṃ rathamāruhya dakṣiṇe ||
svanaṃ gacchati yo maryastasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ || 29 ||
ghoṣaṃ na śṛṇuyātkarṇe jyotirnatre na paśyati ||
śvabhre yo nipatetsvapre tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ || 30 ||
ūrdhvadṛṣṭistathā raktakṛṣṇadṛṣṭiśva yaḥ pumān ||
ūṣmāvihīnadehaśca tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ || 31 ||
nābhau vā hṛdaye vā'pi suṣiraṃ yasya bhāsate ||
yasyātyuṣṇaṃ bhavenmūtraṃ tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ || 32 ||
jāgratkāle'thavā svapne yo'dṛṣṭena nihanyate ||
jīvanaṃ tasya nāstyeva mṛtyuragra iti sthitaḥ || 33 ||
agnau yo nipatetsvapre yo vā naṣṭasmṛtiḥ sadā ||
yāmyaśabdaṃ ca yo brūyāttasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ || 34 ||
śuklaṃ prāvaraṇaṃ raktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vā yasya bhāsate ||
svame nīlaṃ paṭaṃ yasya tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ || 35 ||
evamādīnyariṣṭāni bhāsante yasya dusthitam ||
sa bhayaṃ śokamohau ca tyaktvaikāgramanā dṛḍham || 36 ||
śrīmaddārāṇasīṃ gatvā snātvā gaṅgājale naraḥ ||
dṛṣṭvā viśveśvaraṃ devaṃ japetpañcākṣaraṃ sadā || 37 ||
somanāthe'thavā snātvā somatīrthe mahodadhau ||
somanāthaṃ mahādevaṃ dṛṣṭvā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 38 ||
śrīparvate'thavā devaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrīmallikeśvaram ||
bhasmanonūlya mantreṇa sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 39 ||
śrīkālahastināthaṃ vā suvarṇamukharījale ||
snātvā dṛṣṭvā mahādevaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 40 ||
goparvate tathā devaṃ dṛṣṭvā śaktīśvarābhidham ||
bhasmanoḍhūlya mantreṇa sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 41 ||
śrīmadṛdvācale vā'pi snātvā muktājale naraḥ ||
dṛṣṭvā vṛddhācaleśānaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 42 ||
śrīmadrāmeśvare vā'pi snātvā tatra mahodadhau ||
dṛṣṭvā rāmeśvaraṃ devaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 43 ||
śrīhālāsye'thavā devaṃ dṛṣṭvā hālāsyanāyakam ||
yathāśakti dhanaṃ dattvā sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 44 ||
vedāraṇye'thavā snātvā vedatīrthe mahodadhau ||
vedāraṇyādhipaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 45 ||
śrīmahalmīkasaṃjñe vā kṣīrakuṇḍajale naraḥ ||
snātvā dṛṣṭvā maheśānaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 46 ||
jagāraṇye'thavā snātvā kāveryāmeva mānavaḥ |
gajāraṇyādhipaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 47 ||
japyeśvaraṃ tu vā gatvā snātvā kāverikājale ||
dṛṣṭvā japyeśvareśānaṃ sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 48 ||
athavā dakṣiṇāvarte snātvā kāverikāle ||
dakṣiṇāvartanāśaṃ dṛṣṭvā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 49 ||
kumbhakoṇe'thavā srātvā kāveryāmeva mānavaḥ ||
kumbhakoṇādhipaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 50 ||
madhyārjane vā kāveryāṃ srātvā martyaḥ samāhitaḥ ||
madhyārjanādhipaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 51 ||
śrīmadropatīrthe vā tathā maṅgalavaṃśake ||
śrīmadagnīśvarākhye vā koṭihāsye'thavā naraḥ || 52 ||
āmratīrthe dṛtisthāne vetāraṇyasamāhvaye ||
śrīmadbrahmapure vā'pi kāveryudhisaṃgame || 53 ||
srātvā dattvā yathāśakti dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ tilaṃ tu vā ||
dṛṣṭvā maheśvaraṃ bhaktyā sadā pañcākṣaraṃ japet || 54 ||
athavā mānavaḥ śīghraṃ gatvā vyāghrapuraṃ mudā ||
śivagaṅgābhidhe tīrthe snātvā dattvā yathābalam ||55 ||
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā śrīmaddaśrasabhāpatim ||
dṛṣṭvā pañcākṣaraṃ mantraṃ satāraṃ sarvadā japet || 56 ||
asminvyāghra pure puṇye yo vā ko vā tu mānavaḥ ||
mamāra paramā muktiḥ siddhā tasya na saṃśayaḥ || 57 ||
mahāpātakasaṃghāśca sthānasyāsya praveśanāva |
naśyanti darśanādeva muktiḥ siddhā sabhāpateḥ || 58 ||
mahākāruṇiko devo mahānandaparāyaṇaḥ ||
yatra nṛtyati taṃ dṛṣṭvā mucyate bhavabandhanāt || 59 ||
deśadarśanamātreṇa vimuktā bahavo janāḥ || -
kiṃ punardevadevasya darśanena sabhāpateḥ || 60 ||
avimuktādapi śreṣṭhamidaṃ sthānaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||
atra nṛtyati deveśastatra devo na nṛtyati || 61 ||
atra darśanamātreṇa muktiḥ siddhā hi dehinām ||
tatra naṣṭasya martyasya tataḥ śreṣṭhamidaṃ puram || 62 ||
śrīmadvyāghrapuraṃ muktvā yo vā vārāṇasīṃ gataḥ ||
tatra naṣṭo'pi kaivalyaṃ prāpnuyānnaiva mānavaḥ || 63 ||
pārvatī paramā śaktiḥ śrīmavyāghrapure sadā ||
prakāśate hi vidyābhiḥ saṃvṛtā karuṇāvalāt || 64 ||
sarvavidyālayā devī yatrātīva prakāśate ||
khalu tatra parā muktirataḥ śreṣṭhamidaṃ puram || 65 ||
śivaprasādena hi tatra mucyate || 66 ||
mṛtyusūcakavivaraṇaṃ nāma paṭcatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 46 ||
caka vivaraṇaṃ nāma paṭcatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 46 ||
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi pāpasyākaraṇāya tu ||
bhogāvaśiṣṭapāpānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ munisattamāḥ || 1 ||
brahmahā kṣayarogī syātsurāpaḥ śyāvadantakaḥ ||
svarṇāpahārī kunakhī duśvarmā gurutalpagaḥ || 2 ||
parivādarataḥ paṅgaranthaśva vadhirastathā ||
anukīrtanakṛnmayaḥ kharasvāmī bhavetsadā || 3 ||
gurunindāparo nityamapasmārī nirantaram ||
bhagaṃdarī gurorājñābhaṅgakārī na saṃśayaḥ || 4 ||
gurumātsarya kṛnmaryo vikrimiḥ syānna saṃśayaḥ||
gurvavajñāparastaddacchivadrohī tathā bhavet || 5 ||
guroḥ śuśrūṣaṇe'sako duṣprajñaḥ syāttu mānavaḥ ||
viṣṇudrohī naraḥ sākṣātkṛkalāsatvamāpnuyāt || 6 ||
yo vedapako martyaḥ sa caṇḍālo bhavettathā ||
vedāntadūpakaḥ sākṣātpulkasaḥ syānna saṃśayaḥ || 7 ||
unmatto vedavijñānadūpakaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ ||
rajasvalābhigantā syādantyajātistu mānavaḥ || 8 ||
agrido manujaḥ kuṣṭhī garadana tathaiva ca ||
śastrapāṇistathā martyo rūpya corastu durduraḥ || 9 ||
kūṭakṛnmukharogī syātkūṭasākṣī tathaiva ca ||
kūṭakṛtyasahāyaśva tadupāyaprado'pi ca || 10 ||
akṣirogī bhavennityaṃ bhāryā tyāgī tu mānavaḥ || 11 ||
patnīvahutve tvekasyāṃ ramate paṇḍha eva saḥ ||
annāpahārī mandāgnirjihārogī bhavettathā ||
agrabhuṃggalarogī syānmiṣṭabhukca tathaiva ca || 13 ||
pañcayajñavinirmukto viśvarāho bhavennaraḥ ||
parvamaithunakṛnmartyaḥ pramehī syānna saṃśayaḥ || 14 ||
abhyāgata parityāgī kapolapiṇḍako bhavet ||
tathā'tithiparityāgī bhavennātra vicāraṇā || 15 ||
svātmotkarṣaparo nityaṃ vāmanaḥ paṅgareva ca ||
gonnaścaiva kṛtaghnaśca jātyandhaḥ syānna saṃśayaḥ || 16 ||
niḥsnehakaḥ svabhāryāyāṃ galagaṇḍī bhavennaraḥ ||
veśyā sevāparo martyaśchinnaliṅgo na saṃśayaḥ || 17 ||
piśunaḥ pūtivaktraḥ syānnarastāmrādivikrayī ||
eḍakojagajāśvādivikretā vyādha eva hi || 18 ||
jñānāpahārī mūkaḥ syānmantracorastathaiva ca ||
abhakṣyabhakṣako maryo gaṇḍamālī bhavetsadā || 19 ||
raṅgopajīvī kumatirbhavennātra vicāraṇā ||
andhaḥ pustakacoraḥ syāttathā syāllekhanīharaḥ || 20 ||
sadā puṇyakathākṣepī vakranāso bhavennaraḥ ||
śiṣṭācārasya dharmasya dūpako rākṣaso bhavet || 21 ||
jñānayogagurudeṣṭā vakrāsyo devadūṣakaḥ ||
puṇyakarmapravṛttasya pratipedhī krimirbhavet || 22 ||
devadravyāpahārī syānmanuṣyo vāyubhakṣakaḥ ||
taṭākārāmabhettā syādaṅgahīnastu mānavaḥ || 23 ||
maryādābhedako dāso bhavennātra vicāraṇā ||
paradārābhigāmī tu vātarogī bhavennaraḥ || 24 ||
madhupramehī coṣṭrādigantā nātra vicāraṇā ||
pativratābhigantā tu sūkaraḥ syāttu mānavaḥ || 25 ||
parāpavādanirato vyasanī cālasaḥ sadā ||
atipātakadoṣeṇa bhaveyuḥ krimayo narāḥ || 26 ||
tathā pātakadopeṇa virāho na saṃśayaḥ ||
upapātakadoṣeṇa tathā śvānaḥ sadā naraḥ || 27 ||
pātakairaparaiḥ kṣudrerjāyante kṣudrayoniṣu ||
mahāpātakapūrvaiśva pātakairakhilaiḥ sadā || 28 ||
svasvarūpāparijñānādvadhyate khalu mānavaḥ ||
svasvarūpaparijñānātkarmabhirna sa badhyate || 29 ||
svasvarūpaṃ tu śuddhaṃ hi satataṃ sarvadehinām ||
svasvarūpaṃ tu cinmātraṃ sarvadā sarvadehinām || 30 ||
naiva dehādisaṃghātaḥ paṭavadṛśigocaraḥ ||
dṛśyarūpeṇa yadrūpaṃ dṛśyate dehapūrvakam || 31 ||
tadnātmaiva dṛśyatvādyaditthaṃ tattathā khalu ||
dṛśyatvaṃ dehapūrvasya saṃmataṃ sarvadehinām || 32 ||
svataḥ kartutvamasyāpi vidyate yadi cā''tmanaḥ ||
tarhi darśanarūpeṇa pariṇāmī bhaveddhi saḥ || 37 ||
pariṇāmī na cā''tmā syātsarvathā mṛttikādivat ||
acittvaṃ ca prasajyeta tataścinna hi vidyate || 38 ||
ciddihīnaṃ jaḍa naiva vibhāti munipuṅgavāḥ ||
svataḥ prakāśahīnasya prakāśo nopapadyate || 39 ||
citprakāśātmasaṃbandhādapi cetyaṃ na āsate ||
tasyābhāvāttataśvetyapratītyā bhidyate hi cit ||40||
ciñcideva sadā viprā na dṛśyaiva hi kena cit ||
yā dṛgdṛśyatvahīnā sā sarvadā bhāsate khalu || 41 ||
sā kadācitra bhātīti yadi syānmunipuṅgavāḥ ||
tarhi naiva vibhāṃtīti vibhānaṃ kena sidhyati || 42 ||
na bhātīti vibhānaṃ tu na bhātamiti cenmatam ||
tarhi bhānaṃ hi nābhātaṃ tejjñānaṃ bhānameva hi || 43 ||
bhānaṃ bhānāntareṇaiva na bhāti dvijapuṅgavāḥ ||
bhānarūpeṇa bhānaṃ tu sadaikaṃ na hi tadvayam || 44 ||
bhātaṃ ānaṃ sadā svena bhāsā bhāti na cānyataḥ ||
yatsvayaṃ bhāti tadvānaṃ khalu bhosyasya bhāsakam || 45 ||
ataḥ sarvasya sākṣyasya sākṣibhūtaḥ svayaṃprabhaḥ ||
ātmā sākṣyagatairdharmaiḥ karmabhirna sa badhyate || 46 ||
grūpaṃ dṛśyasaṃvaddhamiti vaktuṃ na śakyate || 47 ||
saṃbandhasyāpi sākṣyatvātsaṃbandho dṛśyavastugaḥ ||
dṛśyabhūtasya rajjvādeḥ khalu dṛṣṭastu saṃgamaḥ || 48 ||
asaṅgo hyayamityevaṃ bravīti ca parā śrutiḥ ||
tasmādātmā tu cidrūpaḥ karmabhirna sa badhyate || 49 ||
cidrūpasyā''tmanaḥ sākṣādvahmatāmāha hi śrutiḥ ||
brahmaṇaḥ karmasaṃbandhābhāvaṃ cā''ha parā śrutiḥ || 50 ||
tathā sati kathaṃ so'yaṃ karmabhirvadhyate budhāḥ ||
tasmādātmā svamohena saṃsārīva prakāśitaḥ || 51 ||
varṇāśramavayovasthāviśeṣānātmavibhramāt
adhyasyāśeṣavedānāṃ niyojyaḥ syānna ca svataḥ || 52 ||
ajñānādanyathā jñānaṃ manuṣyatvādimānayam ||
ātmā tu paramātmā'pi karmabhirbadhyate'vaśaḥ || 53 ||
karmabhirvyavahāre tu baddho'pi svīyamāyayā |
vastutaḥ paramātmā'yaṃ khalu tairna nibadhyate || 54 ||
svātmanaḥ sarvasākṣitvaṃ dehādevrvyatiriktatām ||
brahmatvaṃ ca śruterjñātvā karmabhirna hi vadhyate || 55 ||
sarvasākṣiṇamātmānaṃ varṇāśramavivarjitam ||
brahmarūpatayā paśyanmucyate bhavabandhanāt || 56 ||
ataḥ svātmāparijñānāddehe'haṃbhāvamāśritaḥ ||
karoti sarvaśāstroktaṃ na jñānī na hi saṃśayaḥ || 57 ||
īdṛśī paramā vidyā śāṃkarī bhavanāśinī ||
prasādādeva jantūnāṃ śaktereva hi jāyate || 58 ||
vāguḍūtā parā śaktiryā cidrapā parābhidhā ||
vande tāmaniśaṃ bhaktyā śrīkaṇṭhārdhaśarīriṇīm || 59 ||
icchāsaṃjñā ca yā śaktiḥ paripūrṇaśivodarā ||
vande tāmādareṇaiva mameṣṭaphaladāyinīm || 60 ||
śaktiryā paramā sākṣādvījabhūtā'khilasya ca ||
vande tāmaniśaṃ bhaktyā nakulīśaśivānvitām || 61||
ūrdhvarūpā'pyadhorūpā tathā'dhasthāpi madhyagā ||
madhyarūpā'pi cāntasthā yā tāṃ vande varapradām || 62 ||
vinyāsairvarṇasaṃkṛtairviśvavidyālayātmanā ||
vidyotamānā yā vāci vande tāmādareṇa tu || 63 ||
ekadhā ca dvidhā caiva tathā ṣoḍaśadhā sthitā ||
dvātriṃśadbhedabhinnā ca yā tāṃ vande parātmadām || 64 ||
akārādikṣakārāntairvarṇaratyantanirmalaiḥ ||
aśepaśabdairyā bhāti tāmānandapradāṃ numaḥ || 65 ||
lakṣmīvāgādirūpeṇa nartakīva vibhāti yā ||
tāmādyantavinirmuktāmahaṃ vande varānanām || 66 ||
brahmādyāḥ sthāvarāntāśca yasyā eva samudratāḥ ||
yasyāmeva vilīyante tasyai nityaṃ namo namaḥ || 67 ||
mahadādiviśeṣāntaṃ jagadyasyāḥ samudratam ||
yasyāmeva layaṃ yāti vande tāmambikāmaham || 68 ||
gurumūrtidharāṃ gṛhyāṃ gṛhyavijñānadāyinīm ||
guhyabhaktajanaprītāṃ guhāyāṃ nihitāṃ numaḥ || 69 ||
